Local News

Letter to the National Merchants from the Association for Upholding the Covenant

Expression from Over a Hundred Trade Associations

▲Urging National Merchants to Resist Aggression and Save the Nation

▲Every Word a Tear, Dishonest Merchants Should Be Alert

The Association for Upholding the League of Nations Covenant of this city is organized by over a hundred trade associations throughout the city, with the participation of chambers of commerce from all over the country. Its branches are spread throughout the country, making it the most recent national merchant group for saving the nation. The association, in light of the current international situation and the dishonest merchants who are the black sheep and act as accomplices to the enemy, yesterday specially issued a letter to the national merchants, urging them to jointly shoulder the responsibility of resisting aggression and saving the nation. Every word is filled with tears and the language is extremely solemn. The record is as follows: The Eastern Provinces have fallen for a year now. This association silently observes the psychology of most people; those who are cautious and self-preserving only know to worry privately and sigh. Those who are indifferent still manage their own businesses and accumulate wealth. Even the black sheep among them, taking advantage of the opportunity, pursue personal gain and engage in treachery and impropriety without regard. In the past, Han Feizi said, "A thousand miles of stony fields is considered no land; a hundred years of foolish people is considered no people." How true these words are. It is only because of this unmotivated nation that it has invited this great humiliation unprecedented in history. In the past, King Zhuang of Chu warned his people that disaster was imminent. This association, adhering to the teaching of "cultivating oneself deeply and being lenient in blaming others," also solemnly informs our business community of the disaster of the collapse of buildings and the breaking of rafters. Our country has historically had an excess of imports. Last year, the customs deficit reached over 500 million taels. However, of the 900 million taels of our country's exports, the Northeast accounted for one-third. Now that the Eastern Provinces have been occupied, the loss of export trade will be another 320 million taels. Therefore, some people estimate that this year's international trade will have at least a 1 billion taels import surplus, which is 1.4 billion in silver dollars. Therefore, the Northeast is not only the lifeline of our country's politics and international relations, but also the lifeline of commerce. Recently, since the Northeast Customs was occupied and the government moved the tax collection elsewhere, products such as sorghum, silk, medicinal materials, and soybeans are all taxed as foreign goods. Merchants, burdened with extremely heavy taxes, have even burned the sorghum they transported to Shanghai after returning it. The source of soybeans has also come to a standstill, depleting the last drop of their blood. Commercial stagnation is already an obvious sign. The Eastern Provinces have only been occupied for a year. How can we sustain this going forward? Therefore, our merchants should not think that the occupation of the Eastern Provinces is the government's business, and resisting foreign aggression is the business of all citizens. It must be understood that the power of modern economics sometimes dominates politics and international affairs. The reason why the League of Nations is hesitant and cautious is that the world economy has not yet stabilized and is unwilling to take the risk rashly. In other words, only the power of economics can extinguish militarism, and those who hold the source of economics are our merchants. Therefore, merchants will be the first to suffer from the disaster of the fall of the Eastern Provinces, and merchants should also be the first to bear the responsibility of resisting aggression and saving the nation. If we can firmly implement a "clear fields and empty villages" strategy, preventing invading countries from exchanging goods for our money, then their annual trade will be reversed, their budget will be short, and their public debt will increase. Even if they squeeze the farmers to maintain their warmongering life, they will inevitably suffer internal strife and perish like rotten fish. Moreover, there are still over ten thousand volunteer soldiers in the Eastern Provinces competing with them, giving them no time to rest and no appetite to eat. If our business community can tighten their belts, do their best to assist them, and prevent the volunteer soldiers from suffering from lack of clothing and food in the freezing weather, then long-term containment will also be enough to increase their military expenses and disrupt their finances. Do not say that the situation is set and cannot be reversed. It must be understood that success or failure depends on whether our business community makes efforts or not. Therefore, we encourage our fellow merchants to pursue the following five goals: 1. Uphold the League of Nations Covenant; 2. Maintain territorial integrity; 3. Implement economic blockade; 4. Aid the Northeast volunteer army; 5. Sanction ambitious countries that violate the Covenant and world peace. Strive towards these goals and work together, hoping that with the strength of the masses, the broken but precious land can be restored. Let us encourage each other.

Telegram from the National Lawyers Association

Exposing the Contradictions in the League of Nations Report

The National Lawyers Association of the Republic of China yesterday telegraphed the League of Nations. The original telegram is recorded below: To Dr. Gu, the Chinese representative in Geneva, forwarded to the representatives of the League of Nations for their consideration. The investigation team's report acknowledges that Manchuria is an integral part of Chinese territory, that the September 18th Incident was a pre-planned act by Japan that exceeded the scope of self-defense, and that the organization of Manchukuo was initiated by the Japanese army and civilian officials, not by the free will of the local people. Then, according to Article 10 of the Covenant, there is no other way to resolve the situation except to restore our country's territorial integrity and administrative independence. However, the recommendations made by the team completely contradict the spirit of the Covenant and the facts it recognizes. The Chinese people who respect the law will never recognize it, and we do not want our country's representatives to participate in the discussion of such illegal recommendations. We dare to ask your representatives to base their recommendations on the aforementioned recognized facts, and to propose recommendations that are in line with the Covenant and international justice. The seal of the National Lawyers Association of the Republic of China.

Ding Chao and Li Du Telegraph About the Rebellion of the Liran Warship

▲Killing the Japanese Advisor and Immediately Throwing the Body into the River

▲Unloading a Large Number of Cannons, Guns, Ammunition, and Military Supplies from the Ship

▲Captain Fan Has Great Merit and Should Be Commended by the Central Government

The United Liaison Office of the Northeast Anti-Japanese Armies stationed in Shanghai yesterday received a telegram from Ding Chao and Li Du regarding the details of the rebellion of the puppet army's Liran warship. The original text of the telegram is as follows: "According to a telegram from Brigade Commander Yongcai stationed in Fuyuan Road (the 21st), at 8:00 PM on the 19th of this month, the puppet army's Liran warship arrived in Tongjiang. Yesterday, it returned to Fuyuan. At 6:00 AM this morning, it suddenly turned back and anchored in Tongjiang. Captain Fan Xuen of the ship stated over the phone that our ship had killed two Japanese advisors and thrown their bodies into the river. Two soldiers on the ship were killed, and over 50 crew members on the ship unanimously revolted, and they requested that your brigade commander take them in and protect them." "I immediately informed Captain Liu of the garrison in Tongjiang over the phone to unload all the military supplies from the ship, and leave the empty ship anchored in the section of the Tongjiang River near Qiqihar Town. At the same time, I ordered Captain Liu to properly deploy defenses in preparation for the enemy. Captain Liu then replied by phone that he had followed the order and coordinated with Captain Fan to carry out the task. A total of two flat-trajectory guns, two heavy mortars, and four machine guns were unloaded, along with tens of thousands of rounds of various bullets. Over fifty naval officers and soldiers, each carrying a Liaoning-made Type 38 rifle, obtained twenty rifles. In addition to Captain Fan of Tongjiang escorting various military equipment to a selected site in Santun, Tongjiang to set up defenses, please give instructions. Just as I was about to send a telegram, another telephone report from Tongjiang stated that Captain Yin arrived in Tongjiang on the Jiangping warship at 6:00 PM this evening. Future developments will be reported in a follow-up telegram. It has been confirmed that the officers and soldiers of the ship were able to kill the Japanese and revolt together, which is rare among the navy and is worthy of admiration. It should be commended or forwarded to the central government for commendation to honor their merits and encourage future generations." "According to this information, Captain Fan Xuen has been in contact with our side for a long time and has long intended to return. This time, he resolutely revolted, demonstrating his deep patriotism and understanding of righteousness. In addition to sending a telegram of commendation and ordering the brigade commander to properly organize and comfort the officers and soldiers of the unit, a special telegram is sent for your information (ten omissions)."

The National Disaster Relief Association's Stance on the League of Nations

The National Disaster Relief Association of the Republic of China has recently published its position on the League of Nations investigation report and the resolution of the Eastern Provinces incident, and has also compiled and printed criticisms of the report, which are now on sale. The conclusions are particularly insightful and reasonable, and are specially excerpted below to show the general opinion of the people. The conclusion states: "The content of the report has been reviewed one by one above, and its contradictions and omissions have been pointed out everywhere. Now we want to express to the League of Nations, the people of the world, the government of our country, and the people of the whole country our feelings from all our gains and the opinions formed from our feelings. First, to the League of Nations and the people of the world, the investigation team's report states many facts fairly. Its recommendations are too accommodating to the facts, perhaps because it hopes for peace too eagerly and mediates with painstaking effort. We are also willing to understand, but the report really contains two major shortcomings. Whether these shortcomings are the investigation team's negligence or deliberate evasion, their relationship is very important and makes the report unable to be adopted directly. These are the two shortcomings that the League of Nations and the people of the world who are concerned about resolving the Sino-Japanese dispute must pay attention to. What are they? First, the Eastern Provinces incident is a stage in Japan's policy of aggression, not an accidental event. The source of Japan's policy of aggression is very old. For forty years, it has swallowed Taiwan, cut away the South Manchuria Railway Zone, annexed Korea, leased the Guandong Leased Territory, occupied Qingdao, and coerced the Twenty-One Demands, all in order to expand its territory and promote its rule step by step, in order to dominate all of Asia and dominate the world. This occupation of the Eastern Provinces is just a predetermined step in this consistent policy, not accidental, and will never stop there. Not only are there previous facts that can be ironclad evidence, but Japanese authorities, soldiers, and politicians have either secretly reported to their emperor or announced to their people, and they have not hesitated to say so. Therefore, to ask about the root cause of the Eastern Provinces incident is Japan's policy of aggression. The investigation team described the political development of China and the recent situation of the Eastern Provinces in great detail, believing that it could clarify the background of the Sino-Japanese dispute, and even said that the enthusiasm of anti-foreign propaganda created a special atmosphere at the time of the incident. However, it did not describe the actual situation of Japan's policy of aggression being promoted step by step and the recent aggressive words and actions of Japanese warlords. It did not explore the real core of the problem, but regarded the surrounding results as the cause of the problem, so that those who are concerned about this matter cannot truly understand the origin of the case, and in the future, it will inevitably produce wrong policies. Isn't this a big flaw? Second, the Eastern Provinces incident is the implementation of Japan's policy of aggression, and is by no means a problem of protecting rights and interests. This can be fully proven from the incident itself. The actions of the Japanese army on and after September 18 were by no means self-defense. The Japanese military and political authorities have repeatedly declared that they will not allow the Eastern Provinces to have any political relationship with China again. These are all very clear evidence of the implementation of aggression. Let's not talk too much about it. Let's look at the investigation team's report on Japan's rights and interests in Manchuria, which is not only meticulously maintained, but also expanded and guaranteed in many places. If Japan is really for the protection of rights and interests, it should have been complacent long ago. Why do Japanese authorities scold the report so much and insist on wiping out the entire Chapter Nine and Chapter Ten? It can be seen that Japan wants to annex the Eastern Provinces as a base for dominating all of Asia, which is beyond doubt. Therefore, to resolve the Sino-Japanese Eastern Provinces dispute and maintain permanent peace, the only way is to fundamentally and effectively correct all the actions of Japan that have violated international conventions and arbitrarily carried out aggression, so that it will know that it is difficult to change its traditional policy of aggression. Only then can it be considered resolved. If it is mistaken that Japan is protecting its rights and interests and that it has created the situation in Liaoning through illegal means, even if it does not recognize it all, it recognizes a part of it. Not to mention that Japan is unwilling to accept it because it is against its will, even if it accepts it temporarily, it will know from then on that aggression is effective and that international constraints are ultimately waste paper. It can be more presumptuous and implement its policy of aggression step by step. Where is there any peace to speak of? Where is there any meaning in the existence of the League of Nations? Not only will small and weak countries permanently become the victims of strong countries, but strong countries will also be permanently disturbed by Japan's policy of aggression. This principle is extremely clear, but unfortunately the report and recommendations do not even mention this. Isn't this another big flaw? We believe that for the sake of true world peace, the core of resolving the Eastern Provinces incident lies in curbing Japan's policy of aggression. There is only one way to curb Japan's policy of aggression, which is to absolutely uphold all international conventions and make them fully effective. Therefore, we believe that to resolve the disputes, the following three principles should be strictly followed: 1. The League of Nations should, based on the Covenant and the Nine-Power Treaty and the Non-Aggression Treaty, deny all actions taken by Japan in the Eastern Provinces since September 18, and set a time limit for Japan to withdraw its troops to the original stationing points before September 18. 2. Regarding the disputed topics in the Eastern Provinces, after the aforementioned item is implemented, China and Japan should strictly abide by the existing and effective treaties, negotiate a solution, and adjust their disputes. If there is any unresolved dispute, it should be sent to the League of Nations for public judgment. 3. In order to implement the first two principles, the League of Nations should strictly implement the procedures and means stipulated in Article 15 and Article 16 of the League Covenant. Two: To the government and people of our country, our country has joined the League of Nations and shares the great responsibility of maintaining world peace with various countries. Then, in the case of Japan's invasion of the Eastern Provinces, our country's compliance with the Covenant and its appeal to the League of Nations to correct it is our obligation and cannot be said to be wrong. But we should pay close attention to two levels. First, we should strive to maintain true world peace in accordance with the Covenant, but we should not compromise or evade the Covenant, pretend to be peaceful, and suffer useless sacrifices. Second, it is very worrying whether the authority and strength of the League can be fully exerted. We should put this dangerous national situation in our plans and make practical preparations for self-reliance. Therefore, at the upcoming League of Nations General Assembly, we advocate that our country should, based on facts, strongly explain the past, present, and future of Japan's policy of aggression, so that all countries thoroughly understand that there is only one way to maintain permanent peace, that is, to curb Japan's policy of aggression, and resolutely adopt the three principles we have said above and move towards the right path. As for the facts contained in the report, they can be cited as collateral evidence of Japan's aggression everywhere, and the principles it cites can also be adopted as arguments. However, its recommendations, although they feel that the basic heart is commendable, are expedient measures and cannot achieve true peace. This is not to be blindly followed. What we have always been distressed about is that the government, in addition to taking the road of the League of Nations, never makes a painful effort to prepare for self-reliance and self-defense. It must be known that the League of Nations itself has various difficulties. It is feared that it may not be able to take any effective measures against the Eastern Provinces incident. If it is not prepared again, what is the difference between sitting and waiting for death? Preparation should be made from both diplomatic and national defense aspects. Diplomatically, the United Kingdom and the United States may have the possibility of uniting against Japan, and the United States and Russia may also have the possibility of uniting against Japan. It is up to us to clarify the pros and cons, provide guarantees, and take responsibility in order to promote a new situation. We must not sit idly by. As for national defense, it should be jointly undertaken by the national army, with precise deployment and strict array. No need to talk more about it. However, all these methods have one major premise, which is that the whole country must work together. If the government still firmly adheres to the system of refusing people's cooperation, and the party monopolizes power, and the people still scatter and retain the mind of not being responsible, then everything that is said is completely nonsense. We do not believe that there is a government that wishes to perish the country, and we do not believe that there are people who wish to perish the country. Everyone, wake up quickly and cooperate quickly." (The whole book is distributed by Huatong, Dadong, and other bookstores.)

United Association of National Mass Organizations for National Salvation

Full Text of Appeal to the International Community (Continued)

㈡ Japan's Brutality in Invading China and its Disguises: The Sino-Japanese War of 1894 (1894). Japan declared war on China, plundered land and money, and forced China to sign various unequal treaties. Since then, its aggression against China has become increasingly blatant. Nothing better demonstrates its ambition than the Twenty-One Demands, which it forced Yuan Shikai to recognize in 1915, taking advantage of the raging European War. According to this treaty, China was virtually turned into a Japanese dependency. This is a humiliation that all Chinese people feel deeply ashamed of, and a plan that Japan has never forgotten. Later, the document presented by Tanaka to the Japanese Emperor stated even more clearly that "to conquer the world, we must first conquer China." The September 18th and January 28th Incidents were in fact the implementation of Tanaka's established policy by stubborn Japanese soldiers. Later, Japan sent troops to Jinan, assassinated General Zhang Zuolin, and its desire to annex China became increasingly rampant. During the September 18th Incident, the Japanese army, under the pretext of self-defense, occupied the three northeastern provinces, and then established a state entirely under its control, openly recognizing it in defiance of the world. Can this be called self-defense? Later, it attacked Shanghai without cause, turning the prosperous city in the East into a ghost town. Is this what is meant by self-defense? In total, in the past year, Japan has massacred more than 20,000 Chinese people and destroyed more than 300 billion in property in China. Can such inhumane behavior be called self-defense? In order to disguise its great injustice in establishing the puppet state of Manchukuo, Japan has been propagating to the international community that it is based on the voluntary organization of the people of Manchuria. However, the fact that the volunteer armies in various parts of Manchuria have been resisting automatically for a long time since September 18th is not enough to show the will of the people and reality? This further shows that its disguising words are far from the truth. However, Japan is known to the world for its ability to create rumors and deceive. Therefore, it either calls China an unorganized country, or calls the Soviet movement in China developing, or calls China's boycott of Japanese goods a boycott of foreigners, or says that Japan has an overpopulation and must immigrate. There are endless kinds of disguising propaganda. However, the increasingly organized nature of Chinese politics is an undeniable fact, and it is Japan's imperialist policy that is destroying China's organization. Moreover, assassinations in Japan are endless. How can it claim to be an organized country? Furthermore, the development of communism in China is the result of Japanese aggression. The aggression of Japanese imperialism has bankrupted the majority of the people, made it difficult for China to industrialize, unable to absorb the majority of the poor, and made China's politics unstable, unable to regulate the turmoil of the poor. Japanese imperialism simply refuses to reflect. As for the Chinese people's boycott of Japanese goods, it is an unavoidable punishment for the banditry of Japan. Moreover, this is also a right of conscience for the Chinese people. The Chinese people have never abused this power to other friendly countries. Only to the aggressive Japan is a considerable restraint imposed. People all over the world know the reason for this. In addition, a few Japanese militarists want to cover up their aggression with the pretext of overpopulation, which is even more laborious and clumsy. Even insightful people in Japan recognize this as a kind of unfounded lie. Ironclad statistics prove that the recent population growth rate in Japan has not increased more than before Japan invaded China. Not only that, but Hokkaido in Japan, and Korea and Taiwan, which were seized from China, are also enough to accommodate a large number of people. However, the so-called overpopulation is just a talisman for aggression and an excuse for annexing China's territory. Japanese imperialists have repeatedly declared to the world, "We have no territorial ambitions towards China." However, Japan's actions are always contrary to its promises. What Japan denies is actually its greatest goal. If there is no territorial ambition, why are tens of thousands of troops still stationed in Manchuria? Although the Chinese people are a peace-loving nation, this does not mean that they will not restrain aggressors. The 19th Route Army resisted the 100,000 Japanese troops with 30,000 troops for nearly two months. Finally, out of consideration for the overall situation in the world, it voluntarily withdrew. This alone is enough to prove that Japan's aggression only increases the resistance of the Chinese people. The recent resistance of the volunteer army has not been deterred by Japanese airplanes and poison gas. It can be seen that Japan's ambition to conquer China only increases the contempt and anger of people around the world. ㈢ Regarding the Report of the League of Nations Investigation Commission: The League of Nations Investigation Commission spent several months investigating the dispute between China and Japan. Its hard work is something we are grateful for. In particular, its respect for the Kellogg-Briand Pact in the report and the confirmation of the atrocities of September 18th and the creation of the puppet state, which violated the Kellogg-Briand Pact and the Nine-Power Treaty, can prove that the views held by the Investigation Commission are fair and do not go against the original intention of the League of Nations itself to uphold peace. However, its upholding of peace has not achieved its purpose, and its recommendations are beyond our expectations, which cannot but make us regret the Investigation Commission. Japanese aggressors are dissatisfied with the report because it did not fully support Japan's aggression, and what we are dissatisfied with is that it failed to properly fulfill its mission, and it is still too biased towards the aggressors. First, the Investigation Commission believes that the Chinese people's boycott of Japanese goods is an illegal action and an organized behavior. However, it is not known that it is human nature for a weak country to deeply hate and avoid dealing with the strong and violent, and it is also a means of last resort. No one may interfere with it. As for the so-called organization, it is nothing more than the expression of the entire Chinese people's hatred of the Japanese invasion. Secondly, the Investigation Commission believes that Manchuria should be governed by the international community, leaving only China with a nominal sovereignty. We certainly do not reject China's development and the cooperation of friendly countries. However, this should maintain China's sovereignty in order to prevent endless disputes. After all, the majority of the people in Manchuria are Chinese, and China has the greatest interest there, and it is China's lifeline. China will inevitably maintain its sovereignty, and with the considerable cooperation of various friendly countries, it can unleash the wealth of Manchuria, and the people will also understand this kind of assistance in jointly developing Manchuria. If a so-called advisory council is established to govern Manchuria, then it is feared that the residents there will all feel the pain of national subjugation and will not welcome this new regime, which will only give Japan the greatest opportunity for aggression. Moreover, once this bad precedent is set, it will be tantamount to encouraging the atrocities of aggression. If a country forcefully seizes the land of another country and is not subject to the constraints of the covenant, then it is feared that this kind of behavior will occur more and more, and the future of world peace will be bleak. In summary, the recommendations of the Investigation Commission are tantamount to fundamentally recognizing Japan's past behavior as legitimate, recognizing that Japan has special privileges to invade China, and recognizing the validity of the Twenty-One Demands. This is something that the people of the whole country cannot recognize even if they die ten thousand times. Secondly, they want to replace Japan's monopoly with international co-management. This is also no different from giving Japan the convenience of aggression, and allowing Japan to occupy the largest majority in the advisory council. Such an advisory council is nothing more than Japan's puppet. Various countries have not gained the actual benefits of developing Manchuria, but have helped Japan's aggression. This is the second thing we deeply doubt about the Investigation Commission. The Investigation Commission has a fundamental prejudice, believing that it is impossible to restore the original state of September 18th, and believing that a country's invasion of another country can be recognized as legitimate. Then the weak countries of the world have no guarantee, and the crisis of peace will increase day by day. As for saying that the Manchurian Incident is not an act of aggression by one country against the territory of another country, then the Investigation Commission cannot but be self-contradictory. If Japan's military action cannot be called self-defense, nor is it aggression, then what is it? This is the third thing that the Investigation Commission has failed to make a judgment based on facts. As for whether the various recommendations are beyond the responsibility of the Investigation Commission, we do not want to discuss them in detail. After all, if the recommendations can be fair, they still have great value. If they lose their fairness, even the report is not acceptable. However, the recommendations of the Investigation Commission are feared to only make the arrogance of aggression grow day by day. This is the fourth thing we are uneasy about the report.

㈣ Our Hope for the International Community: Since the Japanese atrocities of September 18th, the Chinese government has been almost without resistance so far. The superficial diplomatic relations between China and Japan have not been severed. This is entirely due to the trust in the League of Nations that it will eventually maintain the sanctity of its covenant and exercise its powers. The people of the country are even more looking forward to the League of Nations Investigation Commission's report after its publication, expressing a very clear judgment internationally and obtaining a just solution. However, because its recommendations have reasons that cannot but make us regret, we feel that the League of Nations Investigation Commission has failed to understand the national character of China in history and the spirit of unity and resolute resistance of the Chinese people. Although the Chinese people have always loved peace, whenever they encounter foreign aggression to an intolerable degree, they will rise up to resist and persevere. Past events are all there, and they are clearly visible. At present, stimulated by Japan's continued violence and aggression, the degree of enthusiasm of the people of the whole country for united resistance is based on the aggressive behavior of the other party, and it increases with the passage of time. All industrial and commercial enterprises within China are affected by this. Other unexpected events and future troubles are still beyond expectation, and they are all caused by Japanese aggression. That is, the various friendly countries and the League of Nations Conference should bear the responsibility and obligation to effectively maintain the covenant and exercise their powers. This is something that we hope from the international community and should not be ignored.

㈤ Conclusion: Therefore, what hinders China's development is Japanese aggression. What has a conspiracy to disrupt the world and threatens world peace is Japanese aggression. Japan has created rumors, saying that the state of Manchukuo is the will of millions of people. In fact, even in Japan, insightful people recognize that Japan's aggressive behavior is inappropriate. However, a few ambitious militarists are arrogant and intend to disrupt peace without scruples. People all over the world, if they want to maintain the peace and happiness of East Asia with the highest justice, should jointly sanction Japan's aggressive behavior and support China's national movement. This kind of movement is the foundation of modern civilization. The Chinese people will welcome the friendly cooperation of various countries and work together to build a new Manchuria and the whole of China. If this is not done, or Japan's unlimited aggression is tolerated, or the bad precedent of co-management is opened up, it will not only be the greatest imprudence, but also the cause of the world's greatest misfortune. (The End)

Today, 4 Million Silver Dollars Are Shipped to the Northeast

▲ Loaded Four Times in Twenty Days

▲ The Total Amount is 12 Million

Recently, cash has been shipped from Shanghai to the Northeast. More than 8 million yuan has been loaded in the past two weeks, and today there is another large batch of 4 million silver dollars, which will continue to be shipped to Fengtian. The details are as follows:

Amount Reported for Shipment: Today's large amount of silver dollars shipped from Shanghai to the Northeast is the fourth batch of exports, totaling 818 boxes, totaling 4,090,000 yuan. Among them, 3,895,000 yuan will be transferred to Fengtian after arriving in Dalian, and another 145,000 yuan will be directly transported to Niuzhuang. Nanrongji in this port reported loading 1,505,000 yuan, Dongshunji reported loading 790,000 yuan, Yongfengli 550,000 yuan, Tongshilong 270,000 yuan, Yishunheng 320,000 yuan, Beihengyi 250,000 yuan, Dongxingcheng Dachanglong 100,000 yuan each, Tiandexiang 60,000 yuan, Bank of China 125,000 yuan, and Dongshunji 20,000 yuan to Yingkou, all loaded on British ships this morning and left Shanghai.

There is still more to come: It has been found that since the 5th of this month, the shipment of silver dollars to the Northeast has started. The first shipment was 1,780,000 yuan, the second shipment was on the 15th, totaling 3,510,000 yuan, and the third shipment was on the 19th, totaling 3,000,000 yuan. Including today's batch, more than 12,000,000 yuan has been shipped in the past 20 days. Nine out of ten shipments were to Fengtian, and only a small part was to Yingkou. It is also heard that there will be a fifth batch of cash shipped to the Northeast within this month, and the amount is also around 3,000,000 yuan. Various customs declaration companies will have to wait until today's batch leaves Shanghai before reporting the shipment. It is also heard that Japanese ships have shipped cash to the Northeast many times, but the amount is not as large.

Northeast Finance: Since our country sealed off the Northeast on September 25th, the people of the country have stopped purchasing miscellaneous grains, soybeans, and oil from the Northeast. In theory, there is no need to transport these millions of national currencies to Fengtian. However, according to those who came to Shanghai from the Northeast, after the Japanese forcibly occupied our Northeast, they embraced the heart of scraping and looting, so they confiscated the cash of various official silver and money institutions in the Northeast. The amount shipped to Japan is more than tens of millions of yuan. Recently, they have even forced the people of the Northeast to use Japanese banknotes, and restricted the use of banknotes from our country's various banks, which is extremely strict. Therefore, various banks have come to the country to transport huge amounts of cash to prepare for the redemption of banknotes.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Incident

Board of Directors Discusses Debt Restructuring: According to the Central News Agency, the Board of Directors of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company held its third regular meeting yesterday afternoon at around 4 pm. The attendees were Liu Hongsheng, Ye Zhuotang, Shi Liangcai, Zhang Shouyong, Zhang Jia'ao, Du Yong, and Yang Ying, seven directors, and Hu Bijiang, Li Ming, Qian Yongming, Hu Yunzhuang, and Sheng Shengyi, five directors. Shi Liangcai chaired the meeting, which adjourned at 6 pm. According to reporters, the most important thing was to discuss the organizational regulations of the Debt Restructuring Committee. As for the date of establishment and the selection of committee members, Zhang Shouyong, the managing director, said after the meeting that the establishment date was set within this week. In addition to Qian Yongming and Li Ming, the drafters of the regulations, the remaining members will be discussed further today before a decision can be made. There will be a total of seven standing committee members, and lawyers and accountants will also be invited to participate. The amendments to the organizational regulations will also need to be reorganized. Chen Weiqing, the chief of the general affairs department of the company, told reporters that the total debt of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is currently known to be more than 19 million taels. As for the details, only one or two key personnel know them clearly. Therefore, after the establishment of the Debt Restructuring Committee, it is necessary to conduct a detailed investigation first before proceeding with the discussion of various restructuring methods.

Managers Take Photos to Preserve Evidence: According to the Daily News, Li Guojie, the former manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, mortgaged 30 million yuan to the American business company Guo Yingye and the Dalai Shipping Company. The company first handed over 700,000 yuan to Li Guojie. Li Guojie tried his best to shirk the responsibility, saying that the money was accepted by Chen Banmu, the former supervisor of the company. However, after the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company actively investigated, Li Guojie's fraud was completely exposed. According to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, the China Business Operations Company obtained several receipts that Li Guojie had actually received. The receipts had five seals, namely the seal of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, the seal of the Board of Directors, the seal of the Chairman of the Board, the seal of the General Manager, and Li Guojie's personal seal. In addition to the two public seals of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Board of Directors, Li Guojie concurrently served as the chairman of the board and the general manager. Therefore, the receipts were handled entirely by Li Guojie. According to the Daily News reporter, the receipts have been photographed by the General Manager's Office and submitted to the Ministry for review.

Will Chen Fumu Return to China as Scheduled? The Minister of Transportation, Zhu Jiahua, repeatedly telegraphed Chen Fumu to Beijing, instructing him to report to the Central Government on the process of mortgaging the four wharves to foreign companies. However, Chen had already gone to Hong Kong in advance. A few days ago, he telegraphed Minister Zhu twice from Hong Kong, stating that borrowing money from the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company was a common practice and did not require prior approval from the Ministry of Transportation. He, as the supervisor, had the power to approve it, and the mortgage had been agreed upon long ago, only signed recently, and the 85% of the funds transferred did not harm the rights of others. He showed defiance towards the government. Therefore, the court has now issued a summons, instructing him to appear in court for questioning. If he does not return to China within the time limit, the National Government will order his arrest. As for Chen's party membership, it will also be proposed for expulsion at the Third Plenary Session next month as a warning.

Another Ship Added to the Sino-European Route

A Giant of 24,000 Tons from a French Company

At the beginning of this month, the new postal ship "Contessa Vittoria" of the Italian company came to China and joined the Sino-European route. It takes 23 days from Shanghai to Italy. This ship can be called the champion of the Sino-European route. Recently, it was heard that the new postal ship "Atsmia" of the French company, with a load of 24,000 tons, will arrive in Shanghai from France this week (i.e., the 26th) and go to Japan next week. After returning to Shanghai, it is scheduled to depart from Shanghai on the 3rd of next month for its maiden voyage to Marseille. It is also heard that the previous voyage of the "Messagerie" ship "Angoulême" from France to China, for some reason, stopped at Saigon, and all passengers and cargo destined for China were transferred to the new ship.

Silk Prices Plummet and Shuang Gong Silk Factory Announces Closure

▲ European and American Market Prices Plunge and No One Advises

▲ Inventory Piles Up and Temporarily Suspended to Await a Turnaround

The Shuang Gong Silk Factory in this city has recently seen a sharp decline in sales in the European and American markets, resulting in a buildup of inventory. The Fulun and Honglun factories, which have been struggling to maintain operations, announced their closure yesterday to wait for an opportunity. The details are as follows:

Difficult to Maintain: There are only seven Shuang Gong Silk Factories in the country, including Fulun in Shanghai. Their business has been in a slump for many years and has reached its limit. Sales in Europe and America have disappeared, and they have been forced to close down one after another. Only the Fulun Shuang Gong Factory at the end of Tianbao Road in Hongkou, with 216 machines, and the Honglun Shuang Gong Factory on Liuying Road in Zhabei, with 204 machines, have been struggling to maintain operations to maintain the livelihood of the workers.

Complete Closure: Recently, due to the continued poor business, the sharp drop in prices in the European and American markets, no one advises, the inventory piles up, and the turnover is not smooth, the Fulun and Honglun factories, which have been struggling to maintain operations since yesterday, have also announced their closure to wait for an opportunity. According to the manager of the factory, there are only two Shuang Gong Silk Factories operating in the city. Recently, the sales of foreign firms have dropped by 50 taels per dan, and there have been no transactions. The price difference is more than 200 taels compared to the previous price, and the cost per dan is huge at the current market price. Moreover, the inventory is piling up, and the closure has been announced.

Pork Industry Opposes the Jiangsu Finance Department's Collection of Pork Tax

▲ Representatives Sent to Shanghai to Form a Joint Office

▲ Telegrams to the Central Departments, Provincial Governments, and Requesting Explicit Orders for Abolition

The fresh pork industry in various counties north of the Yangtze River previously reported that the business tax bureaus of Tongzhou, Rugao, Jingjiang, and Taixing counties had illegally collected pork export taxes at the ports along the river in each county, and had repeatedly telegraphed the relevant departments and provincial governments requesting a ban. Representatives were elected to go to Beijing and the provinces to petition, and the Executive Yuan, Ministry of Finance, and Provincial Government approved the abolition. This matter has come to an end. However, the Department of Finance has now changed the name and appointed Lou Fumin as the Pork Tax Commissioner of Tong, Ru, Tai, and Jing, imitating the previous method of unified pork tax in northern Jiangsu, and scheduled to start collecting taxes on the 25th of this month. The pork butchers in each county believe that this tax is completely a lijin tax, which violates the central government's legal determination to abolish lijin, and they cannot afford it. They have sent representatives to Shanghai to organize a joint office to handle opposition matters. Yesterday, they telegraphed the Executive Yuan, Ministry of Finance, Provincial Government, and Department of Finance, requesting a swift order for abolition. The telegram reads: To the Executive Yuan in Nanjing, the business tax bureaus of Tong, Ru, Jing, and Tai counties in Jiangsu Province set up checkpoints along the river and collected two jiao per pig, which is a heavy tax and causes great trouble to merchants. Petitions were filed separately, and the Yuan, Ministry, and Department issued explicit orders for abolition. The pain of the merchants has not been eliminated, and unexpected disasters have come again. The Department of Finance has appointed Lou Fumin as the Pork Tax Commissioner of Tong, Ru, Tai, and Jing, setting up offices and bureaus, which is a more severe approach. Its method is no different from the central government's explicit order to abolish lijin. It undermines the credibility of the central government and increases the suffering of merchants. We earnestly request the Yuan, Ministry, and Department to quickly issue an order for abolition to relieve the merchants from their suffering. We await orders in great haste.

Opposition to Telephone Price Increase Becomes More Serious

Over 600 More Lines Disconnected

User Association's Attitude: On the issue of the Shanghai Special District's telephone price increase, the telephone company has expressed a firm stance, with no room for compromise or hesitation. Therefore, 570 lines have already been disconnected. Although 200 customers continued to pay and had their lines reconnected, according to a recent survey by the Telephone User Association, as of yesterday, the telephone company continued to disconnect lines, reaching over 100-200 in the Central District and over 400 in the New Central District. Therefore, the situation is becoming more serious. It is reported that the User Association is determined to confront the company, vowing not to yield, and preparing for major sacrifices, while waiting for the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to negotiate with the American Minister to order the company to cancel the price increase.

Taxpayers Association Sends Another Letter: The Shanghai Chinese Taxpayers Association sent a letter to the Public Works Department yesterday, stating: "Dear Sir, according to Shao Renhua (telephone number 4408) in his letter, the telephone price increase issue requires an urgent return to communication. We should write another letter to Mr. Zhong and Mr. He of the Public Concession Public Works Department, urging the company to reconnect first and wait for a solution. Otherwise, not only will deductions be made on a daily basis, but compensation for losses must be heard to be fair. As for the general discussion of the company's position, without clarifying its capital, the amount of goods purchased, equipment expenditures, whether there is any excess, the breadth of the site, and the war losses, regardless of the year, completely requiring existing users to make up for it, how can there be such a reason in the world, etc. Based on this, we request that you investigate and handle the matter as soon as possible." Technician Wang Defa of the center received him, answered various inquiries, agreed to assist in the investigation of the general situation of China's fisheries, and discussed the exchange of publications with the US fisheries authorities in the future. The results were quite satisfactory.

Customs Proclamation on the Sinking Location of the Fuqing Ship

General Directorate of Customs Maritime Department Shipping Proclamation No. 1037, stating: "For the purpose of proclamation, the Director General of Customs has ordered: 'A Fuqing ship has sunk in the Yangtze River Estuary Channel. Its location is directly north of Hengsha Beacon, with a distance of 4.5 nautical miles. The sunken ship's bow is facing northeast, and it is submerged about 19 feet underwater at low tide, tilted to the starboard side at about 20 degrees. The masts and smokestack are all exposed above the water, which is a hindrance to navigation. A lighted buoy should be placed at that location to indicate the location of the sunken ship.' A separate list should be drawn up and the Inspection and Works Department should follow the instructions." It should be complied with. It is hereby proclaimed, and the order is recorded below for all Chinese and foreign shipowners to be informed. Special proclamation (including) ㈠ Location of the Lighted Buoy: The location of the lighted buoy is southwest of the sunken Fuqing ship, about 1.9 nautical miles away. From that location, the bearing to Hengsha Beacon is 3 degrees true north, and the distance is 4.17 nautical miles. ㈡ Lighted Buoy Situation: The lighted buoy is decorated in green and is an intermittent flashing green light, flashing once every eight seconds, with each flash lasting four seconds. ㈢ Related Maps and Books: Hydrographic Chart No. 505 and 1011 of the Ministry of the Navy of the Republic of China. November 19, 1932, signed by Colonel Kanal of the Maritime Department Inspection and Works Department."

Two Cuban Youths' Roaming Feat 37,000 Miles of Car Travel

▲Interesting Tea Party at the American Trading Company Yesterday

Two young men named Bairdi and Bieteira from Cuba, in the prime of their lives, held great ambitions. Last autumn, they drove a Ford car to roam across the United States, starting from Boston, passing through Mexico and Canada, spending ten months, covering a distance of 37,000 miles. They visited almost all the major cities in the 49 states of the United States. Newspapers competed to report their stories, and the automotive industry considered it a beautiful tale. Now, Bairdi and Bieteira have brought their Ford roadster, which has accompanied them on their long journey, to Shanghai for sightseeing. Mr. Bowen, manager of the American Trading Company on Avenue Foch, held a tea party in the company's showroom at 5 p.m. yesterday to show his hospitality and invite Chinese and Western reporters from Shanghai to participate. In addition to displaying the Model A Ford car they drove (see picture), there were also photos taken along the way, newspaper articles, and a map of the itinerary, arranged around for viewing. The car was decorated with badges and flags, almost full, all of which were presented by public and private institutions in various places as proof of their journey. Bairdi and Bieteira gave explanations, which were very interesting. They said that since the departure, the climate and conditions in various places they passed through were different. The heat in Mexico and the cold in Canada differed by more than 100 degrees. In Canada, the road was covered with silver snow, endless white, and the wheels were trapped in the snow, making it difficult to walk. Fortunately, the Ford car was well-made and advanced all the way, with no mechanical difficulties. Bairdi and Bieteira arrived in Vancouver at the end of July this year, then took a boat to Japan, toured the three islands, and traveled through Korea, the three northeastern provinces, Peiping, Tianjin, Nanking, Hankow, etc., to Shanghai. The car they drove had been used briefly ▲Running 37,000 miles ▲

in Shanghai, but in other places, due to road conditions, they were unable to enjoy the driving pleasure. They may try it again in the future.

Yesterday Morning, a Policeman in Nanshi Died While Chasing a Thief Who Robbed Gold Jewelry

▲Ms. Zeng Wang's Gold Necklace Was Robbed

▲The Policeman Held the Thief in His Arms

▲The Thief Urgently Opened Fire on the Police

▲Officer Lu Died in the Hospital Due to Serious Injuries

Yesterday morning, in the territory of the Second Precinct of the First District of Nanshi, a thief robbed a woman's gold jewelry. A policeman bravely chased after the thief and was shot in the abdomen, a vital area, by the thief. He died in the hospital in the afternoon. Details are as follows:

Woman Robbed on the Way: Ms. Zeng Wang, a local woman, 44 years old, residing at No. 17 Yongze Lane, Guangqi Road, went to buy pig's head meat near Fu Jia Lane at around 9 a.m. yesterday. Unexpectedly, on the way, two robbers suddenly appeared, one wearing a blue cloth shirt and pants, and the other wearing a black cloth shirt and pants, blocking her way and threatening her with a gun, forbidding her to make a sound. Ms. Zeng Wang, seeing the situation, knew she had encountered robbers, and was immediately terrified, standing motionless like a wooden chicken. The robbers snatched a gold necklace (worth over one hundred yuan) from her neck and fled separately with the stolen goods. One of the robbers, wearing a blue cloth shirt and pants, turned from Shengjia Lane into Sanpailou and fled.

Policeman Hugged the Thief: At the same time, Lu Chunshan, a policeman from the Second Precinct of the First District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, was going to Sanpailou to relieve Wang Jincai, the guard on duty at the third post. At that time, while passing by the entrance of Guanyitong Lane, he suddenly saw a robber wearing a blue cloth shirt and pants, looking flustered, running from afar, and after being pointed out by passers-by that the person was indeed a robber, Officer Lu immediately went forward and hugged the robber around the waist.

Officer Lu Shot in the Abdomen: The thief, realizing that things were not going well, activated the mechanism of the pistol he was holding and fired two shots. Officer Lu was shot in the lower right abdomen. The thief took the opportunity to struggle free, took steps to escape again, and continued to fire shots backward. Although Officer Lu was injured, he still drew his gun and fired back, and bravely chased after him. However, due to the vital injury and the continuous flow of blood, he fell to the ground after only a few steps.

The Robber Escaped on the Spot: At that time, Wang Jincai, the guard on duty at the nearby third post, also heard the alarm and rushed over. Seeing the thief still running wildly ahead, he also tried to catch up. The thief, in a desperate situation, ran into the back door of the Dai Chunlin Perfume Shop, then rushed out of the front door, went straight to Yimiao Avenue, and then turned into the gate of Yimiao. When Officer Wang tracked him down, there were crowded tourists in the temple and the thief had disappeared.

More Than a Dozen Holes in the Intestines: Soon, the news spread, and the patrol officer led Chief Li and others to search everywhere. In the meantime, the injured policeman Lu Chunshan was sent to the Shanghai Hospital for treatment. After being examined by the doctor, it was said that Officer Lu was shot in the abdomen, and the small and large intestines were pierced by the bullet, resulting in a dozen holes. The bullet did not pass through, and his life was in danger.

Died of Serious Injuries in the Afternoon: The doctor used X-rays to find no trace. Officer Lu was already in a coma and the situation was very dangerous. Director Xu then submitted a request to Director Wen for medical expenses. Unexpectedly, at 5:50 p.m., Officer Lu died of his injuries. Officer Lu was 25 years old, from Hubei, and had served in the Second Precinct of the First District for two years. He was usually very diligent and cautious, and was praised by successive directors. Officer Lu's family still has an elderly mother, a widow, and young children. He was poor after his death. In addition to preparing a coffin, he has submitted a request to the Municipal Public Security Bureau to consider Officer Lu's death in the line of duty and provide preferential treatment. The funeral is scheduled for 2 p.m. today, and all precincts will attend.

Bandits Extort 20,000 Yuan, Threatening Arson

▲The Contact Person Must Wear a Knotted Satin Hat

▲And Must Hold a Red Paper Package as a Sign

▲Detectives Ambush as Agreed

▲Lu Jiangshun, Liu Ruiyan, and Others Were Arrested

Huang Zhangfa, a Cantonese, lives at No. 2, Baolean Road, North Sichuan Road. He works at the Gold Exchange and has accumulated some savings. Recently, he was coveted by bandits. From the 27th of last month to the 22nd of this month, he suddenly received four threatening letters, extorting 30,000 yuan. Huang reported the case to the Disraeli Road Police Station, but no arrest was made. A letter came again the other day, saying that if he continued to ignore them, they would set his house on fire. They requested that at around 1 p.m., someone be sent to the vicinity of the Yunji Hotel at the corner of Guangdong Road and Fujian Road to make contact. The person must wear a knotted satin hat and hold a red paper package as a sign, otherwise they would take drastic measures. Huang was shocked and immediately reported to the police station. The chief sent Detective Mao Yiwen, a Chinese detective, and all the detectives disguised as vendors, along with Huang's representative, Mr. A, dressed as instructed, and went to the agreed location to wait, while other detectives ambushed in all directions to observe the situation. After a while, Lu Jiangshun (25 years old) and Liu Ruiyan (36 years old), both from Tongzhou, arrived leisurely and wandered near the hotel. Suddenly, they saw Huang's representative and went up to ask, "Are you sent by Mr. Huang?" Mr. A said yes. Chen and Liu said that this was not the place to talk and asked him to go to the Great World. Mr. A pretended to agree and nodded frequently. Detective Mao and others of the police station rushed out and arrested Chen and Liu and took them back to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Zhang Tianyin, the police station's lawyer, stated the previous events and said that the two defendants admitted at the police station that they were sent by three other people to make contact at that location. If they obtained the money, they would be paid 20 yuan each, and they did not know anything else. Today, the victim and the representative at the time were not in court, and all the letters are stored at the police station. Please postpone the case for further investigation. Detective Mao then reported the circumstances of the arrest of the two defendants. Judge Zhao Linyu questioned the two defendants about their age, origin, and occupation. According to Daoxian, they were rickshaw pullers, and the remaining statements were evasive. The judge ordered them to be returned to custody and rescheduled for further investigation.

Old Wife Not Dead, Young Beauty Departs

▲ Mao Lianqing Accused of Fraud, Rape

▲ Abandoned After One Year of Cohabitation

▲ Mao Claims Accusations Are Utterly False

▲ Judge Asks for Leave Yesterday, Rescheduling Trial

Mao Lianqing, a Ningbo native and owner of the Mao Jintai Wood Shop at 200 Sichuan Road, is 42 years old. He previously met a local woman, Jiang Ruying, somewhere. Ms. Jiang is 30 years old and of decent appearance. The two immediately took a liking to each other and were mutually attracted. Around the seventh month of the lunar calendar last year, Mao and Ms. Jiang met again at Wing On Company. After talking, their feelings became harmonious, and they went to the Great Eastern Hotel for intimate enjoyment. One night passed quickly, filled with endless romance. The next day, they moved to the New New Hotel and continued to live together. After more than ten days, they built a "golden house" at No. 7 Datong Lane, Baker Road, as a place to keep his beauty. At this time, their love was quite strong and remained so for almost a year without any disagreements. Unexpectedly, recently, for unknown reasons, a storm suddenly arose, and their relationship broke down. Ms. Jiang then hired Zhao Shen and Chen Honglai as lawyers to file a complaint with the First Special District Court, accusing Mao Lianqing of fraud, rape, and malicious abandonment. Her complaint stated that the plaintiff, while purchasing clothing and items at Wing On Company around the seventh month of the lunar calendar last year, happened to meet the defendant Mao Lianqing, who used sweet words to seduce her and diligently offered his affections. He then lured her to room 69 of the Great Eastern Hotel and persuaded her in every way to marry him as his second wife, claiming, "Because my old wife is dead, I have long wanted to marry you. I have already asked someone to be a matchmaker and propose to your mother several times, and she has already agreed. They say that as long as you yourself agree, this marriage will be successful. Since we have met in person today, it can be called a heaven-sent marriage, and we don't need them as matchmakers. So today, I must propose to you. Please agree to me in person, and then I will give you this ring as an engagement gift," etc. As the plaintiff is a woman, her will was weak. At the time, she believed in his sincerity, unaware of his deception, and mistakenly believed that a marital relationship had been established. She then expressed her agreement and requested to have the wedding ceremony before cohabitation, but he insisted that he must first cohabitate until he obtained permission from his mother, and then complete the ceremony. Once his mother agreed, they would complete the ceremony and enter the house. For now, they would temporarily form a small family outside for convenience. Thus, both parties agreed, and the defendant gave her a ring as

Proof of Free Marriage. The next day, the defendant booked room 23 of the New New Hotel, and they cohabitated for more than ten days. At this time, the defendant's love for the plaintiff was very strong. On August 14th, he rented the lower wing of No. 7 Datong Lane, Baker Road, and formally cohabitated. Because the plaintiff was already pregnant, both parties agreed on the plaintiff's living expenses. The defendant admitted to paying 150 yuan per month, which he would pay forever without interruption. For several months, the defendant fulfilled the verbal agreement. Unexpectedly, starting from the end of February this year, for some unknown reason,

The Defendant Stopped Cohabitating, And the Agreed Living Expenses Were Also Not Paid. The plaintiff's private savings were also exhausted, leaving her in a difficult situation and struggling to make a living. On May 20th, the plaintiff's mother asked the defendant for expenses, and he only gave 60 yuan. On June 1st, the plaintiff was admitted to Guangren Hospital for childbirth and gave birth to a son. All medical and recuperation expenses were needed, so she repeatedly sent people to report to the defendant and asked him to pay the expenses. Not only did he disappear and not come to cohabitate, but he also did not give any money. Therefore, after searching everywhere, she finally learned that the defendant's so-called deceased old wife was still alive.

Such a Beginning and Abandonment, Playing with Women, Disregarding the Livelihood of the Plaintiff and Her Son, Thinking of the Future, the Pain is Extreme, (omitted). Based on the above circumstances, the defendant has clearly committed crimes under Articles 244 and 310, paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law, and should be ordered to appear in court to be punished accordingly, and file an incidental civil lawsuit, requesting that the defendant be ordered to pay: (1) 55,500 yuan for the plaintiff's support (calculated at 150 yuan per month, from March of this year to the end of the year when she turns 60); (2) 12,000 yuan for the child's support (50 yuan per month, from June of this year until he turns 20); (3) 3,220 yuan for the child's education expenses (calculated at 100 yuan per year for elementary school from age 7 to 13, but calculated at 360 yuan per year for middle school from age 14 to 20), totaling

70,700 Yuan. Hoping that the court will order the defendant to pay it all at once to punish the unlawful and save women and children, etc. The court approved the complaint and ordered Chinese constable Guo Xiangyao to notify both the plaintiff and defendant to appear in court for questioning. Yesterday afternoon, the scheduled date for the trial arrived. The plaintiff, Mao Jiang Ruying, arrived in court with her lawyer Chen Honglai, while the defendant Mao Lianqing hired lawyer Dai Jien to appear in court, stating that all the plaintiff's accusations were completely false and that the truth would eventually come to light. Later, because the presiding judge Wu Zhen asked for leave due to a matter, the case could not proceed and was rescheduled for the afternoon of the 30th of this month.

Pudong Electricity Fee Continues to Be Reduced

Implemented from January 1st Next Year

The electricity price of the Pudong Electric Company was originally 25 cents per kilowatt-hour. After repeated urging by the Municipal Public Works Bureau, it was gradually reduced to 22 cents per kilowatt-hour in January of the 19th year. In December of the 20th year, the Public Works Bureau signed a contract with the company, stipulating a method for reducing electricity prices annually. The company first reduced it to 21 cents per kilowatt-hour from January 1st of the 20th year. Now, according to the agreement, starting from January 1st next year, it will be reduced by another cent per kilowatt-hour, only charging 20 cents. The electricity price will also be reduced accordingly: (1) If the average monthly electricity consumption per horsepower is less than 150 kilowatt-hours, it will be reduced to 7 cents per kilowatt-hour; (2) If the average monthly electricity consumption per horsepower exceeds 150 kilowatt-hours but is less than 250 kilowatt-hours, it will be reduced to 6.3 cents per kilowatt-hour; (3) If the average monthly electricity consumption per horsepower exceeds 250 kilowatt-hours but is less than 350 kilowatt-hours, it will be reduced to 5.6 cents per kilowatt-hour; (4) If the average monthly electricity consumption per horsepower exceeds 350 kilowatt-hours, it will be 4.6 cents per kilowatt-hour. All these reductions will be implemented at the same time as the electricity price reduction. It is reported that it has been submitted to the Public Works Bureau for record, and by then, the electricity price in Pudong will be not much different from that in the western districts.

Second Phase of War Zone Relief Loans to Open Early Next Month

Total Amount is 100,000 Yuan

The Shanghai Municipal War Zone Relief Committee, in order to revive the war zone and relieve disaster victims, allocated 250,000 yuan for temporary relief loans in the war zone, to be issued in two phases. The first phase, 100,000 yuan, was opened on the 16th of this month and is about to be completed. Only a small number of borrowers have not collected their loans because the procedures have not been completed. According to the War Zone Temporary Relief Loan Office, there are still more than 30 borrowers in the first phase who have not collected their loans. These more than 30 borrowers have generally failed to complete the procedures such as guarantor, so they have not come to collect the loans. It is now planned to end this at the end of this month. If the registered borrowers still do not collect their loans by then, a few more days will be given. If the borrowers still do not come to collect the loans after the deadline, the first phase of loan coupons that have been issued will be invalidated in order to proceed with the second phase of loans. The remaining funds from the first phase that have not been issued will be transferred to the second phase for issuance, so as to avoid confusion in the procedures. The total amount of the second phase of loans is 100,000 yuan, including 27,000 yuan for poor people's loans (9,000 yuan for Zhabei District, and 3,000 yuan each for Zhenru, Jiangwan, Wusong, Yinhang, Yinxiang, and Pengpu districts), 50,000 yuan for house-building loans (distributed according to the original proportions of each district, including 13,000 yuan each for Zhabei, Wusong, and Jiangwan, 2,500 yuan each for Yinhang and Pengpu, 5,000 yuan for Yinxiang, and 1,000 yuan for Zhenru), 20,500 yuan for small industrial loans (distributed according to the original proportions of each district), and 2,500 yuan for porridge distribution. This money can be allocated at the beginning of next month. Once the funds are allocated, the second phase of loans will begin, around the beginning of next month.

▲ All Tram Lines Operating as Usual

▲ Salary Increase Issue to Be Mediated Today

The workers had already accepted the order of the authorities and drove eight trams out of the various lines at 5:00 pm the day before yesterday, operating for one week to indicate the resumption of work. Yesterday morning at 5:00 am, all the workers had arrived at the factory to work, and all the tram lines were operating as usual. The details are as follows:

Resumption of Work Situation: After the general meeting decided to resume work the day before yesterday, starting at 5:00 am yesterday morning, all tram lines were operating as usual. Each tram was still protected by a member of the police brigade. The order was very good, and no other problems occurred at night.

Mediation Today: After all the workers resumed work and restored traffic, only the salary increase issue that had been appealed for had not been resolved. National Coal Relief Association Asks Central Government to Relieve Chinese-Owned Mines

The tax rates for various domestic mines are different. The Sino-foreign joint venture Kailuan Coal Mine only pays one customs duty, one penny of Kai Ping silver per ton, and has no other taxes and levies. However, Chinese-owned coal mines, in addition to paying mining area production and sales taxes and customs duties, also pay various local miscellaneous levies. The burden is heavy, the cost increases, the selling price is slightly higher, and sales are stagnant. The rural economy of our country has already gone bankrupt. If the mines are shut down and the national coal production stops, not only will the number of unemployed people increase sharply, but the national income will also decrease sharply. If it is not rescued as soon as possible, the harm is unthinkable. The National Coal Relief Association in this city, in view of the fact that national coal has been hit by the dumping of Japanese coal and is also facing price competition from Kailuan, which has lower costs, the market is even more declining, and the crisis is lurking. It is reported that it has prepared a document to petition the central government to provide relief to various domestic mines so that the Chinese-owned mines that are on the verge of bankruptcy can survive.

Lin Pengxia Gave a Lecture on Aviation Yesterday

Ms. Lin Pengxia, our country's first female aviator, whose style name is Xiaochong, is from Putian, Fujian. She studied in the United States and also studied aviation in England for many years, making her the earliest Chinese woman to study aviation. This time, she came to Shanghai from Singapore and plans to go to the Northwest for inspection, determined to develop the Northwest through aviation. After Ms. Lin arrived in Shanghai, people from all walks of life welcomed her with great enthusiasm, and she was very busy with social engagements. Yesterday, at the request of various schools, she gave a lecture on aviation. At 9:00 am, she lectured at the Nanyang Commercial High School on Shanzhong Road. The school's principal Wu Xinglian, Dean of Studies Wu Jiangleng, aviator Huang Heqing, and Xu Tongye, a representative of the Aviation Construction Association, as well as teachers and students of the school, attended. Here is a record of her speech: "Everyone knows that aviation has a major relationship with the country. During this national crisis, to save the country, we must study and promote aviation. After the September 18th and January 28th incidents, the Chinese people felt the need for active aviation construction even more. The invention of aircraft was in 1903 and has only 30 years of history. People at that time did not pay attention to it. It was not until 1913 that European and American countries and Japan began to pay attention to it. After the European War, all countries in the world have strived for aviation construction and adopted it for civilian use to facilitate transportation. Military aircraft are also divided into four types: reconnaissance, bombing, expulsion, and combat. The speed of progress is truly amazing. According to the survey statistics of 1928, there were more than 2,000 aircraft, 3,500 air stations, and more than 30,000 pilots in European and American countries. Looking back at our country, there are only more than 20 aircraft and more than 30 pilots. The difference is too great. Because I felt the need for aviation, I decided to study when I was in England. People in that country were very surprised because I was the first Chinese woman to study aviation. Fortunately, I succeeded in my studies and hope to continue my research. The purpose of this trip back to China is to awaken the Chinese people's attention to aviation. We must know that only aviation can consolidate national defense and protect our territory. At this time when the Japanese bandits are advancing step by step, we cannot sit still and wait for death. We should rise up and strengthen ourselves. As for the purpose of this trip to the Northwest for inspection, it is because the provinces of Qinghai, Ningxia, and Suiyuan in the Northwest are rich in products and have vast wastelands, which foreigners have coveted for a long time. We must immediately find ways to develop them. I am willing to contribute to the Chinese people through aviation, regardless of success or failure. I hope that the Chinese people will work together to make efforts," etc. Yesterday morning at 11:00 am, Ms. Lin also lectured at Qingnian Middle School, at 11:30 am at Baiwen Middle School, Huizhong Middle School, at 3:00 pm at Shanghai Middle School, and Minli Girls' Middle School, and in the evening at Liangjiang Women's Physical Education College, etc. It is reported that she will go to the Northwest in a few days.

Urging Factories to Register by Deadline

Ministry of Industry Re-advises Municipal Government Yesterday

The Municipal Government previously instructed the Social Affairs Bureau to handle factory registration in accordance with the Ministry of Industry's request to investigate the situation of various factories in this city. It has been many days, but many factories are still waiting and watching. The Ministry of Industry re-advised the Municipal Government the day before yesterday to expedite the submission of registration forms by the deadline. Therefore, the Municipal Government forwarded the Ministry of Industry's advisory yesterday for compliance. The advisory from the Ministry of Industry is recorded as follows: "Regarding the matter of advising, the Ministry has held factory registration and previously advised your Municipal Government to investigate and instruct the competent authorities to comply and expedite the process of submitting the reports by the deadline, and your Municipal Government was allowed to forward the factories applying for registration to the Ministry for review and separate approval or rejection. However, factory registration focuses on making the situation of factories across the country clear as a whole, without any omissions, so that precise planning can be done to seek the development of industry. Now, it is found that the factories that your city has submitted for registration account for only a small number of the factories in the entire city, so it is difficult to have a comprehensive understanding. Accordingly, we advise you again to investigate and strictly urge and expedite the submission of registration by the deadline for all factories in the city that should be registered, etc."

Wu Song Electric Light Illumination Postponement

Wu Song Bao Ming Electric Light Company, during the war, all its routes were completely destroyed by the Japanese army. Even the factory buildings were bombarded by artillery fire and severely damaged, making it unable to recover. It is now operated by the privately-run Zhabei Water and Electricity Plant. Since the plant took over, it has been working actively. Now, all the routes have been installed. For several days, it has been rushing to repair the houses in the square shed and other machine areas, and it has been roughly completed. Once completed, it is estimated that the illumination can begin at the end of the month or the beginning of next month. All the electric light users in the town have also installed the light wires and are eagerly waiting to turn on the power. Unexpectedly, the Municipal Bureau of Public Works recently sent personnel to Songjiang to inspect the repair work in the factory's machine room, believing it to be unqualified. Because the houses are currently only being repaired, the foundations must not be firm, and there is fear of accidents. All must be rebuilt and the foundations redone before the machines can be installed. Otherwise, the bureau cannot approve the commencement of work. Therefore, the plant's power generation may be delayed, and it will not be able to illuminate for a while.

Municipal Health Bureau Changes Slaughterhouse Inspection Stamps

The Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau is quite strict in its pre- and post-slaughter inspection of pigs, cattle, and sheep. After the pigs, cattle, and sheep are slaughtered, they are inspected by veterinary technicians and then stamped to prevent diseased meat from being mixed into the edible supply. It is now heard that the previously used circular inspection stamps will be invalidated from December 2nd of this year and replaced with triangular inspection stamps. The Public Security Bureau at all district offices has been notified, and orders have been given to all slaughterhouses to comply.
