Datong Music Society Improves Ordinary Silk and Bamboo Instruments

The Shanghai Datong Music Society, after manufacturing large instruments and domestic violins, felt that the decline of national music was still due to the poor quality of ordinary instruments. Because of poor quality, the price is low, but the lower the price, the worse the quality. Now, the society believes that to revitalize national music, it is necessary to improve instruments first. Also, because fewer people study ancient music and more people study ordinary silk and bamboo music, the society takes the improvement of silk and bamboo instruments as a prerequisite. The improved instruments of the society are recorded below: 1) Pipa: The waist of the old-style pipa is too wide, resulting in a lack of high notes. Now, it is changed to a gourd shape, and four more frets can be added to the lower part to increase high notes. It is named the Gourd Pipa. 2) Yueqin: The neck of the old-style yueqin is too short. It has high notes but is not suitable. Now, it is changed to a vase shape, which can increase four high notes. It is named the Vase Qin. 3) Flute: The old method of flute membrane uses a round hole. When blowing a song, it often dries out halfway and the tone changes. Now, it is changed to a long oval hole, with more folds, so it will not dry out for a long time. 4) Low Fourth Guan: According to ordinary silk and bamboo instruments, there are only middle and high ranges. Therefore, when playing a song, it always feels not powerful enough. Now, a low-pitched wind instrument is specially made, its length is equal to the range of the six holes of the dongxiao, and the sound is four times lower than the ordinary sound. Therefore, it is named Double Fourth Guan. Other instruments such as Double Fourth Violin are under research and development and will be available soon.

Mid-River Pirates Rob Cargo Boat

Rascals Take the Opportunity to Collude in Fraud

Chen Zhixin, the owner of the Hengda Yarn Factory in Yangsi Bridge, Pudong, bought 530 bales of used clothing from the Shunfeng Used Clothing Company in Minhang on the 25th of last month, each bale weighing about 120 catties and valued at more than 2,000 yuan. He entrusted the boatman Xue Lansheng to transport them to Shanghai. However, when the boat arrived near Wujiadu, two pirate boats suddenly appeared, with nine bandits on board, each holding a box cannon. They jumped onto the cargo boat, first tying up the boatman Xue Zunsheng and his crew, and then moving all 530 bales of used clothing onto the pirate boats. They were towed by a small steamship directly to the Dingjiazai area of Tangkou, where they sold all the stolen clothing to Ding Caibo, Ding Xitang, Ding Aitang, Ding Bochu, and others who specialized in receiving stolen goods. After each bandit received the money, they divided the loot and fled. Later, after the Hengda factory owner Chen Zhixin learned of this, he reported it to the Municipal Public Security Bureau Water Patrol Team and other agencies, and a reward was offered for their arrest. Now, after investigation, the leader of the detective team, Lu Ying, arrested the key suspect Ding Aitang the day before yesterday. After questioning, he confessed clearly. He immediately led the detectives to Dingjiazai to search, but they had all fled. Only Ding's wife, Sun, was captured. Later, Ding and others entrusted the famous local rascals Tao Shunqing and Cai Afu to intercede with Chen and paid 2,800 yuan to settle the matter. However, Tao and Cai, colluding with the local village chief Ding Ruiqing, falsely accused the farmer Ding Jisheng and his four brothers of being involved in the theft and used threats to extort more than 5,500 yuan. Now that Ding Jisheng and others have learned of this, they have filed a criminal lawsuit with the local court yesterday, accusing Tao and Cai of falsely accusing innocent people of being thieves and extorting money.

Two Russians Rob Foreign Banknotes

Detained and Sent to Police Station for Handling

Recently, one or two Russians have been seen wandering around the Caojiadu area of ​​western Shanghai. When they see that there are only one or two young apprentices in the tobacco and paper shops, they go forward to exchange small coins. They deliberately exchange the small coins repeatedly. When the apprentice takes out a large number of small coins, they immediately grab them and flee. At about 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, at the Tang Yu Mao Tobacco and Paper Shop, No. 861 on Robert Sheng Road, western Shanghai, there happened to be only an apprentice, Chen Rongda, at the counter. Suddenly, a Russian came forward to exchange a foreign banknote for small coins. When he was exchanging the coins again and again, he robbed more than 100 corners (that is, more than 60 coins) and fled. Unexpectedly, at 3:40 PM yesterday afternoon, the Russian came again with an accomplice and broke directly into the counter, claiming to buy Pyramid cigarettes. As the apprentice was reaching for the cigarettes, the Russian stole a 10-yuan banknote from the counter drawer. The apprentice saw it and negotiated with him, but he insisted that it was his own ticket. The owner of the shop, Tang Fuquan, heard the noise and rushed down from the upstairs. The Russian then held the ticket and asked Tang to exchange it for cash. Tang saw that the ticket was indeed from his shop. When he questioned him, the Russian was completely unreasonable. Since Tang could not understand the language and he broke in, it was the apprentice's fault. So he reluctantly endured the loss and went upstairs to get loose money to exchange. Unexpectedly, the Russian followed him upstairs and snatched four 5-yuan banknotes that Tang had taken, putting them back into his sleeve. Tang then thought that he was like a bandit, so he called the police to detain the two Russians and send them to the Sixth District Police Station for investigation.

A Tragedy of Repeated Concubinage

▲ Old Lover Commits Murder

▲ Attempts Suicide After the Crime

Yang Weisui, a 48-year-old native of Nanjing, is engaged in the business of boiling water in a tiger stove in Shanghai. He married a fellow villager, Ms. Sha (34 years old this year), as his wife and rented a room in a pastry shop opposite the Wang family tiger stove in Shipipi Lane, in the city. She had an affair with Yang Sancai (the same age as her), a fellow villager who sells birds in the City God Temple at No. 203 Qinglian Road, Nine Acres. The day before yesterday (the 22nd), Yang Sancai learned that Ms. Sha's husband had returned to his hometown in Nanjing, so he rode to her house in the evening, wanting to continue their affair. When he arrived at Ms. Sha's place, he saw that she was whispering sweet nothings with her second landlord, Yang Agen. Therefore, Yang Sancai was furious with jealousy. That night at 8:00 PM, he went out with Ms. Sha to the Nanyang Inn at No. 337 Minti Yin Road in the French Concession and opened room number five on the third floor. Yang blamed Ms. Sha for continuing to have an affair with the second landlord. Ms. Sha refused to accept this, and the two began to quarrel. Unexpectedly, Yang Sancai was so angry that he had nowhere to vent. He suddenly became murderous and used the razor he was carrying to stab Ms. Sha's throat, face, and right hand three times. Blood flowed like a river. Ms. Sha was injured and fell to the ground, shouting for help. The inn attendant heard the sound and went upstairs to investigate. Yang panicked and jumped out of the window to escape, but he injured his legs and feet and fell to the ground. Knowing that he had caused trouble and fearing punishment, he took the same sharp knife and tried to commit suicide by cutting his throat. People nearby noticed this and rushed to take the knife away. The injuries were still minor. The inn then reported the incident to the Xiafei Road patrol station, which sent detectives to send Ms. Sha and Yang to Renji Hospital for treatment. It is said that Ms. Sha's injuries are very serious, and her life may be in danger.

Barber Sentenced to Murder

Sentence Reduced to Twelve Years Imprisonment

Ding Mingcai, a barber from Zhenjiang, is 53 years old. He used to run a shop in Vladivostok. This time, he came to Shanghai from Vladivostok. On the evening of the 4th of last month, he lured Ma Yuangui, a fellow villager and colleague, to an alley in Yixin Lane on Lao Yong'an Street in the French Concession, pulled out a sharp knife, and stabbed Ma in a vital spot, killing him. He then abandoned the knife and fled. Later, Zhou Shangguang, a Chinese detective from the French patrol station, arrested Ding and sent him to the Second Special District Court. The patrol station lawyer filed a public prosecution according to law. Ding confessed that Ma was too bad, writing a letter to his son-in-law saying that his father and daughter had committed adultery. After receiving the letter, the son-in-law returned his daughter. He had ruined his reputation too much, so he hated him and killed him. The court appointed a lawyer to defend him, declared the defense closed, and waited for the scheduled sentencing. It has been reported in the previous newspaper. Yesterday morning, when the time for sentencing arrived, the patrol station escorted Ding to the court. Wang Gangxu, the chief of the criminal court, presided over the first criminal court and sentenced Ding Mingcai to 12 years of imprisonment for premeditated murder, and deprived him of his civil rights for 12 years. The number of days of detention before the trial was set off against the imprisonment at two days per day. The defendant was transferred back to the detention center.

It is truly a savior for poor women.

Local Constable's Home Robbed

The night before last, around 6:00 PM, the home of Tan Maokun, the local constable of Que San Tu in Zhujiabang, north of Gonghe Xin Road in Zhabei, was raided by several bandits. Two bandits stood guard at the main gate, while the rest watched around the house. Five bandits, each holding a handgun, broke into the inner room, forbidding any noise and driving the family members into one room. They ransacked boxes and chests, stealing clothes, silver dollars, and other valuables worth over 500 yuan. The victim has already reported the incident to the relevant police station, requesting an investigation and arrest.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Shandong coast and the Yangtze River basin would experience cloudy and rainy weather with strong southwest to northwest winds. This is due to a low-pressure system passing through, moving towards the east-northeast or northeast. The coastal area south of Ma'an Island will have clear skies and gentle, variable winds. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the city was 72.0, and the lowest was 52.5. On the same day last year, the highest was 70.7, and the lowest was 52.7.

Education News

Important News

Jiangsu Education Department Orders Restriction on Private Middle Schools Running Normal Schools

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education issued an order to the directors of county education bureaus stating that normal schools are places for cultivating elementary school teachers and should be planned by the provincial and county education administrative organs based on the needs of teachers. Recently, private middle schools have either added normal school courses midway, or run middle schools and normal schools concurrently, regardless of local needs, only using this as a means to attract students, resulting in poor performance. This department has repeatedly prohibited this and requested the Ministry of Education to impose restrictions. All private middle schools that have already been approved to run normal schools may continue to do so, but others are not allowed to run them. The order from the Ministry of Education stated: "Having reviewed the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education's proposed measures to restrict private middle schools from running normal schools, which are deemed very important, we provisionally approve the record pending the promulgation of the Normal School Organization Law by this ministry." Therefore, in addition to distributing this order, it is hereby ordered that the bureau directors be informed and that they pass this order on to the private middle schools under their jurisdiction.

Representatives of Schools in Peiping Petition Again Yesterday

Nanjing, 23rd – Representatives of primary and secondary schools in Peiping continued their petition to the Central Party Headquarters and the financial and education departments of the Executive Yuan on the 23rd. Their submission to the Central Party Headquarters stated that if the central government's allocated funds are not disbursed on time, the primary and secondary schools in Peiping will go bankrupt. In addition, the Peiping Primary School Principals' Conference sent a telegram on the 23rd to comfort the representatives.

News from the Ministry of Education

A summary of recent news from the Ministry of Education is as follows:

(1) To the Ministry of the Interior, regarding the forwarded consultation on the Fujian Provincial Department of Civil Affairs' request for instructions on the establishment of district-level senior elementary schools. A draft was sent for notification. (According to the inquiry from the department, does the previously promulgated uniform method for establishing district-level elementary schools only apply to schools newly established after the establishment of district offices? The Ministry of Education explained that the uniform method for district-level senior elementary schools does not only apply to schools established after the establishment of district offices. It is also applicable to district-level elementary schools established before, which should also be run in accordance with this uniform method.)

(2) A letter to the Ministry of Personnel requesting an investigation and reply on whether current personnel laws and regulations have any provisions regarding foreign degrees, or how they plan to regulate them in the future.

(3) Due to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' request for funds for Consul General Huang in San Francisco to participate in the World Games, a special letter was sent to the Secretariat of the Executive Yuan, requesting it to be forwarded for approval.

(4) The Executive Yuan instructed that the list of debts owed to Southeast University should be included in the domestic and foreign debt consolidation plan and handled accordingly. It was decided that the Jiangsu Provincial Government should still find a way. This is hereby notified.

(5) An order was issued to the Hangzhou Art College, the education departments of Hubei and Jiangsu provinces, and the Shanghai Education Bureau to instruct "the college or forward to" Wuchang Art College, Suzhou Art College, Shanghai Art College, and Xinhua Art College to add practical art courses.

Local

Municipal Education Bureau Orders Unified Graduation Exams for Primary and Secondary Schools Next Summer

▲This Semester Will Still Have Proctored Exams

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order to the primary and secondary schools in the city yesterday stating that, due to the small number of schools starting the semester in the spring and the fact that schools are still in the process of reorganization after the war, the graduation exams for this semester will be postponed and will still be administered by each school after submitting the list of graduating students and the exam schedule to the bureau, which will send personnel to proctor the exams. Unified exams should be held for the graduation exams next semester in accordance with the regulations of the ministry. All schools must teach diligently during normal times in order to achieve impressive results on the exams. This order is hereby issued for compliance.

Cai, Zhao Zuwei, Zeng Jinke, Zhu Zhiming, Chen Dingqing, Liu Yaoguang. Alumni including Shen Dingming and Zhu Daosheng, as well as all faculty, staff, and students of the school, totaling over 1,200 people, gathered together, making it a grand occasion. Chairman of the Board Cai Yuanpei presided over the ceremony. After the formalities, Cai gave a speech, stating that the Art College has been established for 20 years. When a young person reaches the age of 20, they should be independent. In their youth, they are naturally not noticed by society. After many trials and tribulations, relying on the hard work of the mother, Mr. Liu Haisu, they have reached adulthood and begun to work in society and become known to society. Twenty years ago, there were no art schools in China. It was not until 1918 that the National Peiping Art College was established, and not until 1928 that the National West Lake Art School was established. Therefore, our school was the first to be established and has the power to turn the tide of the times in the history of art in our country. Today, everyone recognizes the Art College as the only art school in our country, but even if it becomes the only art school in the world, it should strive to achieve excellence. Therefore, it is hoped that the government and society will do their best to supervise and assist it.蔡

After Cai finished his speech, the school principal, Liu Haisu, reported on the 20-year history of the Art College, stating that the school has been established for 20 years, but China did have fine art. But the new art education began with the school in 1912. At that time, the trend of young people was focused on law and politics, which was also due to the need for changes in national politics at that time. Therefore, the initial students of the Art College's predecessor, the Painting and Art Academy, were very few in number. We feel that the survival of the nation and the rise of the country require the entire activity of art, philosophy, science, and politics. Art is a symbol of the spirit of the times and national characteristics. He then recounted the 20 years of the Art College, which have been a constant struggle in pain. Then, Vice Principal Wang Jiyuan reported on the current situation of the school. Mayor Wu Tiecheng's representative, Xu Peihuang, gave a speech, stating that art and science should advance simultaneously and be carefully promoted so that people can have a fulfilling life, without being biased towards science, and no longer following in the footsteps of Europeans' overly scientific lives. Later, Municipal Party Department representative Mao Xiaxuan, Education Bureau representative Zheng Tan, and guests Chen Qicai, Zhao Zuwei, and Zeng Jinke gave speeches one after another, unanimously praising the Art College's efforts over the past 20 years, which moved all those who listened. Finally, Board Member representative Ye Gongchuo gave a thank-you speech and reported on the plan for future development. Faculty representative Jiang Danshu gave a speech, and student representatives from various schools gave congratulatory speeches. The meeting adjourned at 2:00 PM with music. It is reported that the school will hold an exhibition of recent works by faculty and students at the school on Caishi Road for three days, displaying recent works by faculty and students in over 20 rooms. In addition, an exhibition of calligraphy and paintings by ancient and modern artists will be held at the Chinese Arts and Crafts Society on Avenue Road and the Mingfu Library on Albert Road for ten days, and calligraphy and painting coupons will be issued. By drawing lots with the coupons, one can get a piece of calligraphy and painting masterpiece. Shanghai Municipal Council Considers New School Building Plan

The Yuyuan Road West New School, which the Shanghai Municipal Council plans to build, was previously deemed too expensive. The Public Works Department investigated the situation of other schools and redesigned it. Recently, several acting directors have submitted reports to the Education Committee, arguing that the construction standards of municipal schools should not be lowered. However, in order to save expenses, a revised plan has been proposed to build a school that can accommodate 550 students, requiring 160,000 taels of silver (originally estimated at 250,000 taels). The original plan to build a meeting hall will be abandoned, and the manual arts room will still be located in the existing shed. For meeting needs, there will be four classrooms that can be temporarily connected, which can accommodate 150 students gathering. Land will be reserved for future construction of a meeting hall (estimated cost of 40,000 taels). One committee member stated that they had recently visited the Eastern District Primary School and found that the school's meeting hall was too large and too exquisite. If the Zoujin Nie Zhongcheng Public School needs a meeting hall, they can temporarily borrow it from the public school. The new public school is also close to the Yuyuan Road Girls' School, so it may be possible to borrow it in the future. In addition, it is also possible to eliminate walking corridors in the future construction, and then the acting supervisor of education stated that borrowing the girls' school meeting hall seems difficult to do. In order to save money, the meeting hall can be postponed, but if the school enrolls more than 500 students in the future, it will definitely not be able to accommodate them in a room for 150 people. Therefore, it should still be rebuilt when the economy is slightly better. Another committee member asked if it was possible to cancel the cloakroom and use the corridor for this purpose. The acting director of the Public Works Department replied that the corridor is short and not enough. After discussion, it was decided to ask the Public Works Department to make a model according to the 160,000 plan. The Public Works Department also proposed that there are many school buildings to be built in the future, and it is proposed to form a small committee to review the plans. The committee agreed and elected Dr. Tang and Dr. Ou Yuanhuai to serve as members, along with the acting supervisor of education and the Shanghai Municipal Council's building engineer. The above committee's decision has been approved by the board of directors meeting on the 10th.

Revised Regulations for Introducing Members to This Year's International Race Walking

Facilitate Work, Enhance Interest

| Each Athlete is Allowed Only One Introducing Member |

This year's International Race Walking competition is scheduled to be held on the 4th of next month. In order to facilitate the work of the referees and to enhance the interest in the competition, the itinerary committee has specially formulated several new regulations applicable to introducing members, which will be implemented this year. Listed below:

(1) From the starting point to the Bailinan Road section (intersection of Jessfield Road and Bailinan Road), introducing members are not allowed to accompany the athletes.

(2) Each athlete is allowed only one introducing member. From the Bailinan Road section to the eight-mile point, another introducing member can be changed at that time.

(3) From the eight-mile point onwards, introducing members can be rotated.

(4) Each athlete is allowed only one introducing member at a time.

(5) Introducing members are only allowed to walk or use bicycles.

(6) Introducing members may clear the way and guide the athletes when necessary. However, when an athlete is overtaking others, they must pass from the other side.

(7) Introducing members must not touch the athlete's body when providing drinks, otherwise, they will be disqualified.

(8) Each athlete will be issued two introducing member armbands for rotation. The numbers will be the same as the athlete's. For example, if athlete number one is competing, there will be a number one introducing member waiting at the Bailinan Road section, and a number one B introducing member will replace them at the eight-mile point.

Jiangnan University Football Game Scheduled to Be Held in Shanghai

Chizhi College Forfeits Due to Inability to Form a Team

The football championship competition of the Jiangnan University Sports Association is scheduled to begin next week. In the schedule, Nanjing Central University was originally scheduled to play Guanghua on November 19th and Jinan on December 10th, both of which should be held in Shanghai. It is now learned that Central University cannot come to Shanghai on time due to schoolwork reasons and has agreed with the above two schools to change the dates to December 26th against Guanghua and December 28th against Jinan, held at the original locations. In addition, Chizhi College has voluntarily forfeited all games due to its inability to form a team.

Youth Association Prepares Heated Swimming

Ling Xitao, director of the Sports Department of the Sichuan Youth Association, and Yu Binqi, chairman of the Chinese Swimming Research Association, are aware of the scarcity of swimming pools established by Chinese people in Shanghai, and the lack of sources for producing swimming talent. Although several swimming pools are open every year during the hot summer months for comrades to practice and compete, they are closed as soon as late autumn arrives and the weather turns cold. Many people who are interested in practicing stop because the water is cold. When summer comes again next year, they go back into the water, and the results of what they learned last year are forgotten. Therefore, the time for learning is only three months out of the year, while the time spent neglecting it occupies three-quarters, preventing those who are interested from making progress. Now, Ling and Yu plan to gather swimming comrades in Shanghai and raise preparatory funds to install a water heater in the swimming pool of the Chinese Youth Association on Sichuan Road, so that there will be a continuous training opportunity throughout the year to cultivate swimming talent. It is heard that they are actively proceeding and will soon solicit members.

New Basketball Techniques (3) (5) (Not Allowed) (Reprinted)

—Original by Claire Burcky, Translated by Zhang Guoxun and Qian Yiqin

The Northwestern University basketball team in the United States was the champion of the Ten Giants Tournament in 1913 and also a dominant force. This different key tactic is used to defeat individual defense. It is said that coach Dutch Donborg trains his team to use this method, from a fixed formation.

Number one will pass the ball to number four, number three and number five will cross the left and right sides of the court. Number three will first pass in front of number four, blocking number five's defender. Number five will then closely curve past number four, receive number four's pass, and directly advance to the basket to shoot.

Otherwise, number one can pass the ball to number three, and then follow up, blocking number three's defender, giving number three the opportunity to dribble to the free throw area arc. Number three will then pass the ball to number five, who is penetrating the end of the court. At this time, number five's defender is again blocked.

Free Talk

Quotations from Ma Xiangbo, a Ninety-Three-Year-Old

Hoping for the Illumination of the "Eternal Supreme Wisdom"

— Jing Ji

The Elder Xiang made the following observation when commenting on Chinese and foreign philosophers:

"I feel that among the early Confucians, there was no philosopher like Aristotle! Not even Plato's ideal!

Confucius's life was very noble, but 'the Master's discourse on nature and the Way of Heaven was not to be heard,' as recorded by his disciples. The Master himself said, 'If I hear the Way in the morning, I can die content in the evening!' What Way is this, that one would be willing to die content after hearing it in the morning? It can be seen that this Way is truly precious.

Lao Tzu's Way that can be spoken is not the constant Way; fortunately, there is a 'constant' character; heaven and earth are long-lasting, constantly naturally silent | perhaps he originally came to China from Asia Minor; therefore, in his later years, he went west again through the Hangu Pass to return; otherwise, why go west? Liezi claimed that there were sages in the West, who is this referring to, the Savior?

The ancient Jews looked forward to the Savior, as if hoping for the year, as detailed in the Old Testament.

Plato knew what is called Being; because there are many small existences, he knew that there is an absolute existence; from this unique existence, there is 'all' existence. According to the Chinese 'all' two characters, did they exist in ancient times? Or did they come from the Catholic classics of the late Ming Dynasty? I cannot decide; I remain doubtful!

The great philosopher is, after all, Aristotle, who lived more than 2,300 years ago, not only excelled in logic but also spoke of investigating things; he laid the various foundations of science, and his theories still influence us today. His philosophy relied on the organization and expansion of St. Thomas. According to historical records, in his old age and love of learning, at the time of his death, he earnestly prayed to the Creator, saying: Hoping for the illumination of the "eternal supreme wisdom"!

Aristotle's great spirit, in this one sentence, will endure forever!"

Cold and Heat

| The Contradictory Nature of the Times |

— Fu Hongliao

After a gust of autumn wind blew tighter, the winter clothes that had been separated for a long time were blown onto the body one by one. The rich abandoned the old and chose new ones, while the poor only circled in front of the longevity store. Coldness welled up from the heart; warmth, new clothes, wearing them on the body is relatively warmer than old ones, the same autumn, the same in Shanghai, cold and heat, fully dividing into two phenomena, | poverty and wealth!

The same wind, in autumn and winter, attacking the body would make people feel panicked. On the road, I walked slowly, and facing my jacket that still had a breath, I couldn't help but respond with a sympathetic sigh. Walking, I walked forward with my head down, and a young woman came towards me, her snow-white fox fur coat wrapping her entire snake-like body, only revealing a moving little face, snow-white, a quick longing flashed in my mind;

"......According to reports......the north is bitterly cold, and it snows in late autumn, the anti-Japanese warriors, trembling with guns, only need sufficient clothing......"

The Incomplete World

— Fang Tian

The world is ultimately incomplete. The first is the limitation of life. | Although scientists have invented longevity wine (as reported), it is only for the rich to enjoy, and it can only extend life by ten years. After ten years, one cannot avoid returning to the yellow earth. This is the first major defect of life. The second defect is that youth cannot be permanent, so that general modern ladies, middle-aged women, although people are not old, their appearance has declined, and they have to borrow lead rouge. This artificial difficulty is difficult to defeat natural, chicken skin above, making red and white patches, like the characters in Journey to the West, is very frightening. If you look in the mirror, you can't help but sigh three times at the mirror. This is the second major defect of life. Next, the prosperity of Shanghai is the best in the country. Logically, this Paris of the East should be a paradise on earth. However, there are beggars wandering on the streets, robbers robbing on the road, brothels and meat shops stand in great numbers, and smoke dens and gambling places are everywhere, showing the morbid state of society everywhere. Civilization and depravity are standing opposite each other, a great view in history. Make the wives and ladies of general wealthy families, often be wary, not dare to wear all the treasures at home, as much as possible, walking down the street, this can also be regarded as a pity. In addition, the Far East was originally very calm, but Japan insisted on provoking war; a modern lady walking on the road, encounters a beggar who does not know the situation, especially nails behind her, all such things, it is difficult to finish citing examples, so I will stop here. In short, this is an incomplete world.

I thought, such a wind, probably the snow outside the customs is even greater, those soldiers holding guns, the top is floating like powder snow, the whole body is buried in the snow white inside the child: so I also looked at the woman wearing a snow-white fox fur coat, cast a final line of sight, two snow-white shadows, found out at the same time, cold and heat, two clear contrasts, my body shuddered!

Thoughts are so likely to attack people's weaknesses, after one impression fades, quickly another runs to this head. Remember, this was several months ago, when the weather was still very sweaty, and everyone was enthusiastically donating money to the anti-Japanese volunteer army in the northeast, turning over the newspaper every day. At that time, I thought like this, assuming that everyone was donating so enthusiastically, the temperature was as hot as the weather, but it would not disappear, this amazing donation, how much more spectacular! However, the autumn wind has risen, and a gust of wind has blown everyone's hands into their pockets, so the donations seen in the newspaper are as rare as the dawn stars when the sky is about to dawn. When it's hot, everyone is so happy, when it's cold, everyone is also as bleak as the cold weather. Cold, needs clothing, heat... People are following the weather · Especially the Chinese. Cold and heat, fully expressing a kind of era disease of the Chinese people, in the middle of cold and heat, you can see the psychology of the general people |

Teahouse in Name Only

| Unique Atmosphere of Taixian County |

— Yun Sun

In any place, the place with the teahouse signboard is always the stronghold of general tea masters; only our Taixian teahouse is in name only. Smaller teahouses, at least selling snacks is the main body of their business, medium-sized brands, in addition to selling snacks, also sell a kind of chicken juice soup noodles: their organization, can make outsiders, dare not be the host, the names are numerous, the tricks are varied, teach you no way to deal with, tea leaves to bring their own, brewing water is the waiter's extra money; for example, if you want to drink wine, there are wine vendors, drinking and tea, there is a bowl of dried silk, this dried silk is cooked, with sesame oil, soy sauce, shrimp, shrimp rice mixed, its taste is very beautiful | dried silk with eat with increase, see customers usually reward the small account how much, to determine the number of times to add dried silk; this scene, is the opening play of eating tea, the original is to eat snacks, eat chicken juice noodles, this snack, is the steamed bun made of flour, because it is steamed on the cage, also called "small cage", with crab yellow diced meat to make the filling, the noodle soup is chicken juice fish stewed, there are over the bridge, clear soup and other names: for example, two bowls of noodles, it is called two eight points, each eight points, there is a pot of crucian carp outside, called pouring head, its quality is crisp and fragrant | Jiangnan rarely has this kind of production method: a tea meal finished eating, calculate the money, the principal, the small account, wring the towel, pack the water smoke, separate categories, one by one expenditure, the tea meal account book, take the seat as a unit, also called compartment, if this second seat in this room, it is called compartment two: the people who patronize, commenting, talking about business, the owner please partners, apprentices worshiping masters, all eat a tea, compared to eating some light of the reward, please eat a tea, clearly go to eat steamed buns and noodles, but said: is "go to the teahouse" do not eat steamed buns and noodles, usually there is a satirical saying: teach to do "eating tea do not eat snacks, but there is a big appearance yeah;" just as the Shanghai people say: spiritedly, like something is wrong, if the reader to Taixian to go, if someone gives you such a slip, "by invitation tomorrow morning nine o'clock a tea party in a certain teahouse, wu xi gladden but is fortunate." You must not only take it as tasting tea, you must first clear the accumulated goods, ready to eat a full meal.

Such as the city north's Bin Garden, Sheng Chang, Wan Hua Lou, Ju Le Yuan, also sell Chinese lunch and dinner, generation package feast, furnishings seats, are beautiful and grand, not like a monotonous teahouse; the real teahouse, only one shop called "Guang Sheng Ju", is the market of Lu Chen industry union; in the oppressive summer heat, Zhongshan Park also sells clear tea, is a place for modern men and women to enjoy the cool during the summer vacation, they are drunk with no intention of tea.

The Crossroads of Death (2)(10)(3)

— Fan Yanqiao

Alas! She is our child bride, naturally there is nothing to miss, I am the only seed here, how can I harden my heart, leave my parents who gave birth to me and raised me, and not even leak a message to them? But saving a dinner, thinking that in the happy family economy (illegible), only the heavenly pumpkin can fill the (illegible) village economy collapsed, living here, waiting for old, death, what does it mean? These thoughts, then there is no second distraction enough to disturb his will, and then yearn to the heart.

After making up his mind, he felt that everything in front of him was bright. What is there to miss about such a big pumpkin! Let the parents do it! Rather than giving them the pain of life oppression, how about giving them the wandering son's despondency?

Before the sun was completely swallowed by the horizon, they ate dinner, because they could save a lamp, usually A Gen ate at least three bowls, this evening "effort to add meals", only eat one bowl and a half. Liu Da did not pay attention, Liu Pozi was very careful, and asked:

'A Gen! Are you feeling well today? One and a half bowls is enough'?

"Comfortable", thought for a while, and then said: "Just went to the front village, ate a glutinous rice dumpling at Jiang Niupi's house".

Liu Da heard the three words Jiang Niupi, the boss was not happy, deeply strange son to associate with this kind of person, could not help but say:

'Jiang Niupi is unconscionable, his parents are long gone, thanks to his aunt, raising him to adulthood, in the previous years, secretly ran away, ran to nowhere, not even sending a letter, I always thought that such unconscionable people, must do cannon fodder, who knows that he is still alive, also thinking of home, how many money to bring back? Afraid that I can't live, come to force my aunt to (illegible)' He did not scold A Gen, why to associate with Jiang Niupi! But this seat of words, has implied to A Gen, should be far away and avoid it. A Gen originally wanted to tell Jiang Niupi about his experience, say some out, prove that these years in the outside struggle, already had a grasp, although a platoon leader, has surpassed the situation of Liu Da's son A Gen. But Jiang Niupi is still a Jiang Niupi, did not show the situation of the platoon leader, how can make people believe it. Therefore also swallowed, did not say.

Liu Pozi did not know where to hear the news, said:

'Old man! You don't know yet! Jiang Ersaozi is going to be an old princess."

Liu Da laughed, almost spitting out a mouthful of rice, hurriedly put down the rice bowl, wipe the short beard, put on a funny face said:

'Could it be a dream? Who became an official? Even if Jiang Niupi became an official, there is no such good conscience; with such a good conscience, it is not Jiang Niupi.

This kind of logical law containing philosophy, directly made people speechless, but Liu Pozi still has the courage, citing the scriptures to argue with him:

'Generals and ministers have no seeds, men should be self-reliant. There are also farmers who become emperors, isn't Zhu Taizu "watching cattle"?'

Commercial News

A GlimPSE OF FINANCIAL Activity Amidst the busyness

In recent days, the market has felt vigorous due to brisk customer sales of Changmao [a type of commodity]. Small firms engaged in spot transactions are all extremely busy and overwhelmed with trivial matters. The stock on hand in this district is substantial, so there is a large volume of sales, but the commission rate hasn’t moved. It's likely that this favorable situation can be expected to be a long-term consolidation, and there won't be any more drastic drops. The tight money situation seems to be the standard state of affairs, so it remains unchanged recently. Minor coin fluctuations are also slight, but copper coins fluctuate a bit more.

(Commission Firm, Premium Rate Slightly High) The "Foreign Commission" rate in the early market was slightly lower than the previous afternoon by .375, at 7 qian, 1 fen, 2 li, 8 hao, 7 hu, 5 si. In the afternoon market, due to excessive bullish sentiment, it continued to rise, reaching the previous afternoon's original price of 7 qian, 1 fen, 3 li, 2 hao, 5 si. The "Silver Discount" was the same in both the morning and afternoon markets, at 4 fen, an improvement of 2 fen from the previous day. The surcharge remained consistently a "blank surcharge" because the backing for silver was exceptionally abundant, and banks were also issuing funds, so there was no reason for any adulteration.

(Small Coins Down, Copper Coins Up) Jiangnan small silver coins were down a small half li in the early market, at 6 qian, 1 fen, 7 li. The afternoon market was down another small li, at 6 qian, 1 fen, 6 li. As a result, the two markets were down a total of 1.5 li. Transaction volume was 9,000 jiao in the early market and 5,000 jiao in the afternoon market. Guangdong small silver coins were also down a small half li in the early market, at 6 qian, 1 fen, 6 li. The afternoon market was unchanged. However, the Jiangnan jiao and Guangdong jiao prices were equivalent on that day, which was an unusual market price. Transaction volume was 125,000 jiao in the early market and 25,000 jiao in the afternoon market. Copper coins suddenly rose by 3,000 cash, to 399 cash. Transaction volume was over 37,500 strings, with a total value of 9,400 taels.

(Busy Inflow and Outflow of Silver and Foreign Currencies) News of the bank's receipt and disbursement of "Silver Funds" yesterday was slightly busier than the previous day. Chinese merchants deposited 2.45 million to 2.5 million taels, foreign merchants deposited 2.55 million to 2.6 million taels, various commodity exchange tax revenues amounted to 1.01 million taels, special deposits amounted to 2.7 million to 2.8 million taels, collateral transactions amounted to over 1.3 million taels, telegraphic transfers amounted to 500,000 taels, warehouse withdrawals amounted to 1.2 million taels, and receipts from money shops and silver brokers amounted to over 3.11 million taels. Surcharge receipts amounted to over 410,000 taels, receipts from various remittances amounted to over 700,000 taels, and cash receipts amounted to over 100,000 taels. The "Foreign Currency" exchange and transfer of funds in the early market reached 1.355 million taels, and 870,000 taels in the afternoon market. Banknote transactions were 60,000 taels in the early market and 65,000 taels in the afternoon market. Off-exchange banknote transactions were 120,000 taels in the early market and 90,000 taels in the afternoon market. Voucher transactions were 55,000 taels in the early market and 40,000 taels in the afternoon market. Banks bought actual funds, interbank trading was 1.25 million taels in the early market and 850,000 taels in the afternoon market. Money shops and foreign exchange brokers collected over 3.11 million taels, surcharge receipts amounted to over 220,000 taels, interbank lending of foreign currency amounted to over 2.4 million taels, foreign currency collateral transactions amounted to over 900,000 taels, and transactions of small money shops with customers amounted to over 1.2 million taels.

A WEAK GOLD MARKET

(Minor Changes Caused by Confusing International News) Yesterday's market had few changes and a relatively flat downward trend. However, conflicting international news caused hesitation. From morning to afternoon, there was a difference of two to three taels. Ultimately, compared to the previous day, it fell by 2.3 taels. Various firms competed for supply, and the price fluctuated around 760 taels. The gold market weakened at the opening, showing an unusual trend. The British pound rose while the U.S. dollar fell. Although forward prices fell, the base remained strong, which had an impact. Later, news came from abroad that Italy was considering repaying its U.S. debt, and buyers continued to purchase, returning to the 60-tael level. However, although the foreign exchange rate showed a slight contraction, the internal situation was not tight, mainly because sellers were active on the surface. There was also news that war debts might be delayed, so the market price softened again, ultimately falling back below 60 taels. There were very few swap transactions, and the premium was generally above 6 taels. Due to the market being closed on Wednesday, the conditions of the previous market are recorded below.

(Underlying Downward Trend, Falling by 2.3 Taels) The January opening price was 759 taels and 9 qian, a drop of 1.9 taels. (Before the opening, the gray market for goods was still stable, around 60 taels). Subsequently, due to stimulating news, it immediately broke through 60 taels. Furthermore, due to the scramble to purchase by firms such as Dadecheng, Hengchang, Yongyifeng, and Yongzhaofengchang, it continued to rise by 2 taels, reaching 62 taels. However, the exchange rate for British pounds and U.S. dollars seemed to loosen. Maihang [a firm] offered March at 1.975, while the brokers Chuan Gen offered February U.S. dollars at $29.6875. In addition, Yuanmao, Yongheng, Yuzhifeng, Yongyuhe, Yuanxing, Yongfutaiheng, and others sold over one tael of Leeson, at 60 taels and 4 qian. It was then learned that HSBC had reduced both British and U.S. exchange rates by .125 each. Furthermore, Great Britain made a forward purchase of March exchange at 3.28125. At 9:30, it was 61 taels and a half. Subsequently, it was peaceful, but Huabi offered December U.S. dollars at .4375 and March at .6875, and the price turned soft again. Yuanmao, Yongzhaofengchang, Qianchangxiang, Yuantai, Yuanchun, Zhifeng, Yongchengfengyong and others heavily sold, resulting in a decrease of 2 taels, to 59 taels and a half at 10:00. Shortly after, firms such as Dadecheng, Yuantai, Yuanheng, Yifengyong bought, so it rose by one tael, to 60 taels and 7 qian at around 10:10. Moments later, Hengyu, Chengfengyong, Wanxing, and general retail investors sold, and it was also rumored that U.S. President Hoover and Roosevelt were discussing a plan to postpone war debts, which might be resolved, and sentiment seemed soft. The price fell slightly by over one tael, reaching 59 taels at nearly 11:00. In an instant, Bingxing, Yifengyong, Hengyu, and Fuxingyong bought, and Andar absorbed February U.S. dollars at .6875. At 11:15, it was 60 taels and 8 qian. Afterwards, there were fluctuations of several qian to one tael, but there were more suppliers. It is estimated that Hongli, Hengyongyuhe, and Yifengyong Tongtaichang and others disposed of goods, but the exchange market was peaceful. At noon, it closed at 59 taels and 2 qian, then closed at 59 taels and 5 qian, a decrease of 2.3 taels compared to the previous day. According to the half-day, the maximum was 62 taels and the minimum was 59 taels, a difference of 3 taels. The naked premium was estimated to be 15.5 taels to 16 taels. Yingfengheng and others concluded one or two flat trades.

(Quoted Price Mostly Suppressed by Six Taels) The quoted price for the U.S. dollar was reduced by .125, resulting in 824 taels, a suppression of 63 or 4 taels, which was 6 taels more than the previous day. Registration prices: November 67 taels, December 66 taels, January 60 taels, replenishment water 66 taels.

(Inflow and Outflow of Various Firms Not Heated) Trading on the surface was normal. According to statistics, Fuxingyong, Yifengyong, Zhaofengchang, Yongfeng, Hengchangyong, Yuanheng, Yuanmaoyong and others all bought, while Yuankangxiang, Hengyu, Zhifengyong, Qianchangxiang, Futaiheng, Hongli, Yuhe, and Taifengcheng all sold. Dadecheng, Wanxing, Yuantai, Shunli, and Yuanxingyong had mixed transactions. The Dalian gang sold a total of over 200 contracts, buying over 100. The Guangdong gang had very few transactions. The total amount of contracts for various firms, up to the previous day, was approximately over 18,000.

Nominal Contraction, Actual Release of Foreign Exchange

Yesterday in the gold market, the British pound rose and the U.S. dollar fell, while the exchange rate of British pounds against U.S. dollars continued to decline. The decline of the U.S. dollar against the British pound eased slightly and rebounded. However, the trend of foreign exchange in this port was slightly different: nominally contracted, but actually released. Both British and U.S. exchange rates were reduced by .125, and the rest were also consistently reduced. However, Hong Kong remained unchanged. This was the bank's transaction price. The British pound was initially flat and then stable, ultimately rising by .0625 compared to the previous day. Transactions were no more than several tens of thousands of pounds. The gold firms settled slightly. The U.S. dollar initially stabilized and then declined, fluctuating in a circle, but without much change. Ultimately, it was similar to the previous day, with approximately 400,000 to 500,000 taels traded. The inflow and outflow of gold merchants were not significant, without any major movements. It is estimated that Da Zheng made forward purchases of British and U.S. exchange rates, purchasing March U.S. dollars at $29.75 and selling shillings at 1.975 (Fuchang sold off), equivalent to U.S. silver at $3.2825. Seven-Year Long-Term Bonds Rise by Six and a Half Yuan

|20 Series Consolidated Salt Tax Bonds Rise by Six or Seven Jiao|

|Other Changes Minor, Market Conditions Brisk|

Yesterday (the 23rd) at the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange, futures trading was only not conducted for 96 Financial forward contracts. All other current and next-month contracts were open for trading. Trading was active, and sentiment was lively. However, there were few spot transactions. Market sentiment was unsettled, and demand and supply varied, so prices fluctuated. There was a change of over one yuan between the early and late markets. The early morning buying was stronger, and prices continued to rise by about five or six jiao uniformly compared to the previous day. Afterwards, selling prevailed in the market due to high prices, hovering and falling, so the two afternoon sessions were the lowest periods. However, the closing rebounded due to large investors buying in, and selling pressure eased slightly, resulting in renewed strength. As a result, it was similar to the early morning, with 20 Series Consolidated Salt Tax, Customs Tax, and other bonds continuing to rise by about six or seven jiao compared to the previous day. Others fluctuated up and down, with amounts only around two or three jiao. Financial bonds rose by eight jiao, and seven-year long-term spot bonds, which had not been traded for a long time, rose by as much as six and a half yuan compared to late last month. Furthermore, the futures trading volume yesterday was over 6.6 million in the morning session and over 4.4 million yuan in the afternoon session, for a total of 10,895,000 yuan. Among them, Salt Tax and 20 Series bonds were the most traded, reaching over 1.9 million each. Spot transactions only totaled 26,500 yuan.

Cotton Yarn Market After Bulls Cut Losses

|Overseas Cotton Still Weak, Spot Sales Hopeless|

The yarn market has softened, and the situation is weakening again. Overseas cotton markets are still weak, and there is no hope for the development of actual demand. As a result, sentiment is depressed. Some buyers, seeing the poor environment, are cutting their long positions, and the market is declining. In short, spot yarn sales are too sluggish, and short sellers all have spot goods in hand. All factories are very willing to open, it is said.

(People's Standard Down Six or Seven Qian) At the opening of the People's Standard market, the situation was weak again. Due to a lack of buyers in the market, all months fell by three, four, two, and six qian. The situation was even weaker in the afternoon market, with all accounts falling by 1.2.2 qian. The market rebounded when it closed. The total volume for the day was 17,200 bales. It was found that Mingde sold 800 bales, Changfeng sold 4,400 bales, and Dejiang sold 1,050 bales. (South Shanghai) Yesterday, the number of sources from various routes was not large, about 30. The outgoing routes in this district were initially slack and then active, the situation was one of steady decline. 500 shi of Bo Dao went upstream, and the price rose by half a jiao. Bian Yin Yuan liquor merchants were not active, retail transactions were also light, and market prices were slightly weak.

(Xinzha) Yesterday, there were 25 or 26 boats from Xianglu. The city and rural shops were more active than the previous market. Changxi Beigeng's sudden price increase was allowed. Zhongguan Jiangyin rice opened with a set price. Both early and late rice arrivals and sales were flat, and the market had no ups and downs. The total volume for the day was 3,500 shi.

Dinggan Passenger Rice Arrivals and Sales Both Strong

|Foreign Rice Production Prices Loose|

Yesterday, only one foreign rice wholesale market was open for business, in this district. 100 bags of Saigon rice were still priced at 8 yuan. The stock of foreign rice is still more than 600,000 bags, but most of it cannot be sampled in the market due to issues with collateral and unresolved disputes, so circulation is not high. Owners remained steadfast. As for production area prices, due to slow sales recently, prices have also gradually fallen. Telegrams from Needgong only show 3.6 or 7 qian, and Saigon is slightly over 4 taels. Including expenses, the equivalent Shanghai price is between 8 and 9 yuan. Such low prices in the production area have not been seen for many years, but even at the equivalent Shanghai price, it is still difficult to calculate. Furthermore, due to the abundance of inventory and sluggish sales, there is no hope for orders.

Hunan and Jiangxi passenger rice continue to arrive daily. Yesterday, about 5,000 new bags arrived and were sampled in the market. Recently, passenger traffic has been very active, and the southern route Fuzhou and Quanzhou gangs have been eagerly handling it, with a large appetite. Yesterday, the Quanzhou gang's appetite was slightly weaker, but the Fuzhou gang was active again. The appetite of the Shandong and Hebei provinces on the northern route was even better, because rice prices were cheaper than flour prices. Yesterday, 206 bags of Jiangxi Ji Yuan were opened, priced at 9 yuan and 9 jiao. 640 bags of Ji Wan were also opened, priced at 8 yuan, 6 jiao, 3 fen to 8 yuan, 5 jiao. 200 bags of Hunan Ji Yuan were priced at 10 yuan and 5 jiao, and 1,200 bags of Ji You were priced at 8 yuan, 8 jiao, 8 fen to 8 yuan, 5 jiao. 200 bags of Ji Jinggang rice were priced at 8 yuan, 2 jiao, 3 fen, and 800 bags of Ji Red Rice were priced at 8 yuan and 5 fen, for a total of 3,546 bags, which were distributed by the northern and Fujian gangs, it is said.

Low Transaction Volume in the Flour Market

|Bulls and Bears Both Observing|

Yesterday in the flour market, after the opening in the morning and afternoon, each month generally showed a circling pattern. The quoted price of foreign wheat improved by about one or two jiao. However, the sentiment of both buyers and sellers was mostly to wait and see. The northern small rivers have already frozen, and the large rivers have not yet stopped traffic. At this time, flour sales cannot be strong, so the passenger gangs have no desire to continue to move. On the factory side, sales are not easy, and customers are also inactive and tend to wait and see, with no intention of selling. The current month is approaching delivery, and Fufeng is showing signs of buying in. There are few transactions in the forward months. The total volume for the day was sluggish. It is said that only around 140,000 bags were traded, indicating that both sides are rejecting each other. As a result, this month improved by 2.5 li compared to the previous day, January declined by small 2.5 li, April gained larger 2.5 li, and there were no other changes.

Dull Wheat Futures Market

|This Month Still Firm Due to Approaching Delivery|

Yesterday, after the opening in the morning and afternoon, each month generally showed a state of dullness. This month is approaching delivery, and due to the scarcity of spot goods and limited deliveries, the bulls still felt firm. The opening price was flat in the morning, and it improved by two fen in the afternoon. Trading was abnormally sluggish in other months, making comparisons impossible. However, due to the improvement of foreign wheat prices, sentiment was tight. Months such as February, March and April improved by one or two fen compared to this week, but there were not many chips, and it was difficult for both sides to develop.

North-South Goods, Orchid Seeds High-Quality Goods Coming Soon

|Land Prices Have Already Risen|

Recently, due to a lack of continued arrivals of orchid seeds, market inventories are gradually becoming scarce. It has been found that high-quality goods with good body, color, luster, aroma, and rich flavor have already run out of stock. There are still cheaper goods available in central villages, and sales are showing a rising trend. According to letters from production areas, winter ice goods, though continuing to come out, are not large in number, and good goods have risen by three or four yuan. They are expected to be shipped to Shanghai next week, and the asking prices are bound to increase at that time, it is said.

Silk and Tea, Foreign Firms, Silk Market Dull and Lifeless

Yesterday in the local foreign firm silk market, the market was increasingly dull. Since the change in the exchange market, overseas silk markets have generally cleared

丨Two Seasons of Cocoons Coexist, Over 16,000 Bundles丨

Since the resumption of work in various silk factories in Wuxi, all have been striving for production. However, the sales of foreign silk have weakened again. The cost of imported white silk factories has seen declines with no increases. All manufacturers believe the cost of raw silk is insufficient and are unwilling to sell at a loss. Therefore, silk inventories have increased significantly. Various manufacturers have no interest in purchasing dried cocoon materials. The cocoon market has become increasingly sluggish, with substantial dried cocoon inventories. Warehouses throughout the county reportedly hold over 16,000 bundles of spring and autumn cocoons.

Domestic Factories’ Pearl Tea Sales Show Slight Movement

Yesterday, the "Shrimp Eye" pearl tea produced by local tea factories in Shanghai saw renewed activity. Due to receiving orders from Morocco, the British firm TONG FOO began procuring it. Over 400 boxes were traded throughout the city. The opening market price was from forty to forty-three taels, four to five taels lower than previously. Some sparse transactions of "Precious Eyebrow" and "Needle Eyebrow" teas from the LUZHUANG brand were also made by BAOCHANG and JINLONG trading houses. Except for "Needle Eyebrow," which remained firm, the market prices of other teas were difficult to maintain.

The Most Popular Woolen Fabrics Recently

The price fluctuations of woolen fabrics have varied recently, with some rising sharply due to shortages. Among the most popular are riding breeches, followed by genuine horsehair sleeves and women's solid-colored overcoat wool. Those who have these goods are eagerly hoarding them, considering them rare commodities, as the market supply is extremely short and sales are brisk. Those waiting to buy do not mind the high prices and are purchasing them regardless. The average price of the above three types of goods has risen by more than one-tenth of a silver dollar. Other items, such as Hanling Peng (套頭呢之漢令蓬), leather-faced double cloth (皮面兩布), and pre-made Western-style overcoat wool (預等西裝大衣呢), and leopard-skin wool (豹皮羢) are also showing good trends.

Supplement to the *Shenbao* Local Edition

Discourse

Amnesia

— Buddha

According to yesterday's report, "In the United States, there is a patient suffering from amnesia who has even forgotten his beloved wife and nephew. This person is Colonel Robbins, a famous social economist. Today, when his wife arrived, after entering the room, Mr. Robbins called himself Rogers. Although he exchanged greetings with Mrs. Robbins, he did not recognize her as his wife." This made me think of our country where someone moved his family and forgot his wife. I once laughed and said that this must not be true and was not credible. Now, seeing Rogers not recognizing his wife and children, it is truly an example of things happening in the world. It may not be something ancient people made up.

Furthermore, I think that the disease of amnesia is not only something that ancient people had, nor is it just something that happens in the United States. Even now, many people in our country suffer from amnesia, and very few do not. Foreigners laugh at our countrymen for having "five-minute heat," which shows that our countrymen only have a five-minute memory. After this, everything is either forgotten. Not only can one forget one's beloved wife, but one can also forget the country, forget the vengeance for one's father, and forget one's own life and property. Looking at our country, once a national humiliation occurs, a slogan of economic severance, etc., will immediately emerge. But how long does it last? It soon vanishes like smoke. The deepening of amnesia is truly unparalleled in our country.

Literature & Art

Sentiments at the Year's End

— Chen Baoren

Roaming the lakes and seas, my enthusiasm has waned, unable to bear the year's end as a traveler on the riverbank. The outbreak of war has shattered my heart, and talk of human relationships chills my bones. The vicissitudes of the nation and family are shocking transformations, and the shattered rivers and mountains, who will complete them? Saddened, I gaze north at the many misty trees, and rising to dance at the crowing of the rooster, my tears are not yet dry.

Evening Vista

Alarmed by the days of the raging sea, my aspirations to serve the country are difficult to fulfill. Withered in the setting sun of the western wind, a few sounds of broken-hearted pounding of the washing stone.

Sleeplessness

The short lamp and flickering candle are lonely and boring, and the sound of night rain outside the curtain is rustling. I stroke my pillow, unable to sleep for no reason, and the cold quilt is as hard as iron, bearing the deep night.

Common Knowledge

Points to Note When Using a Stove

— Zhi

After reading Renjun's "On Gas Poisoning and First Aid," I offer these points to those who use stoves.

The cold and frightening winter, especially on days of wind and snow, who doesn't like to gather around the stove for warmth? But how do they know that when the windows are tightly closed and the stove fire is roaring, the lack of oxygen causes carbon dioxide to be reduced to carbon monoxide? This colorless and odorless gas, when inhaled into the body, often leads to fatal danger. Therefore, it is best not to have a stove in winter. If you must have one, you should follow the following points to avoid danger.

1. The stove must have a chimney. Because after coal burns, carbon dioxide is produced. If it is not dispersed outside through a chimney, the coal stove will continue to burn, and it will be reduced to carbon monoxide. Carbon monoxide will not turn into carbon dioxide in air lacking oxygen. If we inhale this gas into the human body, it will combine with hemoglobin in the blood and become carboxyhemoglobin. Because hemoglobin originally has the function of transporting oxygen to supply heat to the human body, once it changes, the exchange of carbon and oxygen in the body makes breathing hurried, from hurried to difficult, and from difficult to stopping. When breathing stops, life is cut off. Therefore, anyone who wants to have a stove for warmth must have a chimney.

2. A pot of clean water must be placed on the stove. Because after the coal in the stove burns, the indoor air will definitely be dry, which can cause diseases of the skin and mucous membranes, such as rhinitis and laryngitis. With a pot of clean water, the steam of the water can humidify the air and regulate dryness.

3. Keep the windows open. Because the chimney's ability is only to send the carbon dioxide and other substances produced after burning out of the room. If the windows are tightly closed, the indoor air is limited, and the oxygen in the air is also limited. The burning of coal relies on oxygen, and at the same time, oxygen is for human combustion. When the oxygen is used up, fresh air from outside cannot enter the room, and the carbon in the room cannot be discharged outside. The result is the same danger.

In the past, many people in various places died from coal stove gas poisoning, which was nothing more than the above reasons. Therefore, everyone, it is better not to have a stove. If you want to have one, you must strictly abide by the above points to avoid dying in vain. Everyone, remember!

Several Essays

— Wenbing

(1) The Story of the Rice Bowl

Yesterday, I ran into Mr. D at the North Railway Station, whom I had not seen for a whole year. He asked me abruptly, "How are you?" "I'm fine, but bread is a bit of a problem. How about you?" "As for me, I only have a rice bowl left." He said humorously, "This makes me confused. What exactly happened?" "You know that I used to live on Baoshan Road. When the January 28th Incident broke out, I escaped as a naked man. Later, when the Japanese devils retreated, I went back to take a look. All my belongings had turned into a pile of ashes. After rummaging through it, I only found a rice bowl that I used at school. It was so heartbreaking! Fortunately, just as the enemy was burning and killing, our Mr. × came to power. Later, my uncle also got a position at this station. So, I took the only rice bowl I had and squeezed in." "Ah, your rice bowl is still valuable! Although...although..." He nodded hastily and went to the station.

(2) Dock Fist

Elementary school students, Shi E acts as a modern school beauty, a combination of Chinese and Western styles, a young master style, athlete's attire, and Western-style college students.

The clothing of our country's students has no fixed rules. Everyone freely wears casual clothes, which has become such a disorganized phenomenon.

Everyone knows that Shanghai has many idlers who specialize in finding business opportunities in the streets and alleys, docks, and stations. They are most active when foreign ships arrive at the dock. There are policemen stationed at the dock, so they don't dare to be too presumptuous. However, most of the carriages and horses are always parked on the opposite side of the dock. Passengers hand over their luggage to the coachmen, and just as they are about to get into the carriage, two or three idlers will suddenly pop out and say fiercely, "Be sensible and quickly hand over the dock fee, or we'll use a gun!" In this way, countless countrymen have been extorted by them. Mr. Guan came from Hankou last week, and idlers surrounded him. Fortunately, he wasn't stupid, and a policeman arrived, so he only suffered a beating. Now, every time I meet Mr. Guan, he always says, "The idlers' dock fist really hurts."

(3) White Russian Beggars

It is said that there are more than 9,000 White Russians stranded in Shanghai. Apart from a portion who rely on public buses and tram strikes to搶搶开车的生意, and apart from a portion who sell felt carpets and soap, the rest can only beg in the streets. The Chinese are very generous. I have seen some coolies throw them several copper coins, probably because they are "foreigners." Yesterday, I walked past Datong Road and suddenly encountered two of them. They said, "You are Chinese, I am Russian. Chinese and Russians are the same!" Then, they said softly, "Please give me a copper coin!" I was furious and said, "You used to be Russian dignitaries. Do you know about the Treaty of Ili between China and Russia?" They walked away, muttering a lot of Russian.

(4) Younger Brother Supports Older Brother

Generally speaking, a person who is severely disabled, or is blind and deaf, or has a broken hand and is lame, or whose whole body is simply born like a turtle, is undoubtedly a consumer of society. How can he talk about helping others? A few days ago, I passed by Sampan New Bridge and discovered a disabled person who looked like a turtle. His hands and feet were less than a foot long, and his head was no more than a large pear. He was sleeping in a cradle, and a tall and strong person was pushing him from door to door to beg for food. The pusher was his older brother, who lived his entire life by relying on his disabled younger brother. This can be considered "younger brother supporting older brother."

About Almanacs

— Tianfang

"Every family uses it, you can't buy it in China."

"Opening-year new almanac, buy one for eight coppers." Hearing the speculative vendors shouting to sell old and new almanacs on the road made me realize that the light of this year had come to an end. The words "old almanac" made me feel that human inertia was difficult to eradicate.

In a feudal society, in China where the rural economy was the foundation, what dominated the minds of most people was not the philosophy of Laozi and Zhuangzi, nor the classics of Confucianism, let alone any new doctrines, but an almanac. A person uses it from birth until old age. No, they still have to use it after death for funerals, burials, and ancestral rites. In short, apart from birth and death, where one cannot freely choose a good day as the two major flaws, other actions must always consult the almanac to pick a perfect day. For weddings, birthdays, building houses, and raising beams, one must of course look at the auspicious and inauspicious days. Even for haircuts, baths, seeking wealth, and traveling, one must choose an auspicious day. This is the only classic among all groups of people who have lost confidence. Therefore, the almanac is a popular textbook of superstition. Correspondingly, there are strange phenomena such as fortune-telling witchcraft. Because if the almanac did not have those stems, branches, five elements, Buddhist birthdays, auspicious and inauspicious omens, etc., then those who rely on this to make a living would lose the basis for their activities. This is not without benefit to the upward movement of society. Regarding the superstition of almanacs, I once saw the following story in a notebook:

Someone named Jia was very superstitious. No matter what he did, he would check the almanac for auspicious and inauspicious omens to determine whether to go or stay. One day, a relative's family had an important matter that required him to be there. However, after checking the almanac, it happened to be a day that was not suitable for traveling. Fortunately, he thought of a way. He climbed out of the wall, thinking that as long as I didn't go out through the gate, I could avoid the taboo. However, the dilapidated wall, coupled with days of rain, was not very strong. Before he could climb over, the wall had already collapsed, crushing Jia underneath. At this time, his son heard the sound and rushed over to help, using a hoe to rake away the loose bricks that were pressing on Jia. However, although Jia was pressed under the loose bricks, his mind was very clear. He gasped and shouted to his son,

"Wait...wait a moment! Please...first go...check...the almanac...to see...if...we can move earth...today..."

Although this is a joke, people who believe in the almanac do indeed have this kind of devotion. I record it here for amusement.

The Answer of the Vase

— Yiping

|Why Be a Vase?|

Since female employees were hired in the capital's agencies, many publications and supplements have discussed it extensively. And their conclusion is: why be a "vase?" The supporting side says that this is the beginning of women's employment. Since men and women are equal, they can of course work in the same agency. However, women are relatively weaker, so their work cannot advance as fast as men's. The opposing side says why don't women do other things well and want to put on makeup and dress up like butterflies, providing entertainment for the big managers.

Yesterday I met a former classmate of mine, she was the captain of the basketball team in school, and had the reputation of "healthy beauty girl", but after a year away, she has changed from the dress of short skirt and basketball shoes to a modern woman in long robes and high leather heels. We talked from school life to the current level of life, and learned that she is also a vase in a certain company, so I wanted to find my answer and asked her: "Why be a vase?"

"We also know the meaning of the capitalists": she replied to me, "They want to use our appearance to call on customers, didn't the Parker department of a certain company become crowded after hiring female employees? Also, when the managers are bored, they can use us for entertainment, haven't there been news of a certain minister forcibly kissing a female employee? This is of course a shame for our women, you see there are many women who rush to it now, and they are all educated to a middle school level, but onlookers should also think from the opposite side, are we women not afraid of shame? (exceptions aside) Also for the problem of bread, if there is a proper career, I think our women may not all be willing to be "vases", let me give an analogy, like many middle school graduates like you, also for the problem of overcrowding in society, they have to sell their writing to make a living, to put it badly, they are "literary beggars", but why are there so many people willing to be "literary beggars"? In short, it's all for the problem of bread."

I have organized her words into the above answer. I hope that the insulting name of "vase" will no longer be found anywhere, especially for our writing comrades, if they want to write something about "vase", they should think that they are also "literary beggars" who are looked down upon by others.

Random Writings

— Xiaoniu

Students are unwilling to yield to others in two places: one is in sports on the playground, where no one lets anyone go first; the other is eating in the dining hall, where no one lets anyone have more chopsticks. These two places are proving grounds for students' abilities.

The toilets in schools are the central mechanism for students' freedom of publication. Their critical remarks about teachers and classmates can be seen on the walls of these toilets, such as slogans like "Down with ×× rice bucket" and "××× bastard."

The discipline department of a school is like a police station, and the discipline officer is like a patrolling policeman. His cold face makes students fearful upon seeing him, as if he is about to devour them. Therefore, some people say that this kind of discipline is the spirit of a teacher combined with law.

Students who are good at sports often show off their skills on the sports field; students who are good at writing often vent their frustrations in newspapers. These are both ways for modern students to show off.

Many teachers, apart from the few hours they spend in class for money and can see students, disappear quietly with their briefcases as soon as the bell rings, irresponsibly, and have nothing to do with students. These teachers see teaching as a business, not as a task.

When teachers meet students on the street, they always look down or turn their heads away, pretending not to have seen them. If a student gives him a bow from afar, he has already seen it, and gives a forced, half-smiling nod. Haha.
